- [Exercise overhead dumbbell triceps extension](exercise-overhead-dumbbell-triceps-extension.md) — Overhead dumbbell triceps extension — triceps brachii strength for passing power, shot-blocking position, and overhead basketball actions [S11, p.2-3].
- [Exercise front plank](exercise-front-plank.md) — Front plank — foundational isometric core exercise for basketball athletes targeting transversus abdominis, rectus abdominis, multifidus, and erector spinae [S11, Ch.8].
- [Exercise v up](exercise-v-up.md) — V-up — dynamic full-range core exercise for basketball targeting rectus abdominis, transverse abdominis, and iliopsoas — simultaneous arm and leg lift to full hip flexion [S11, Ch.8].
- [Exercise side rotational v up](exercise-side-rotational-v-up.md) — Side Rotational V-Up — rotational dynamic core exercise targeting rectus abdominis, obliques, and iliopsoas — simultaneous contralateral arm-leg lift from a side-lying hip-rotated position [S11, Ch.8].
- [Exercise deadbug](exercise-deadbug.md) — Deadbug — stability ball-assisted isometric/dynamic core exercise: contralateral limb extensions while maintaining full lumbar contact with the floor — builds deep core stability for basketball [S11, Ch.8].
- [Exercise side plank](exercise-side-plank.md) — Side plank — lateral isometric core exercise targeting quadratus lumborum, obliques, and spinal stabilizers — key injury-prevention and lateral force-resistance exercise for basketball [S11, Ch.8].
- [Exercise birddog plank](exercise-birddog-plank.md) — Birddog plank — prone plank with contralateral arm-leg extension: trains anti-rotation core stability and gluteus maximus while maintaining a rigid plank position [S11, Ch.8].
- [Exercise pallof press variations](exercise-pallof-press-variations.md) — Pallof press and variations (standing, lateral step, overhead) — cable anti-rotation core exercises for basketball: isometric resistance to rotational force in athletic and defensive stances [S11, Ch.8].
- [Drill standing pallof overhead press](drill-standing-pallof-overhead-press.md) — Standing Pallof overhead press — anti-rotation + anti-lateral-flexion core exercise for basketball players, with lateral step variation.
- [Drill elevated bridge hold](drill-elevated-bridge-hold.md) — Elevated bridge hold — glute/posterior chain isometric exercise with feet on bench; alternating leg lift variation builds single-leg hip stability for jumping and driving.
- [Drill reverse hip extension hold](drill-reverse-hip-extension-hold.md) — Reverse hip extension hold — prone bench posterior chain isometric for glutes/erectors; Bosch single-leg variation builds unilateral hip stability for basketball athletes.
- [Drill wood chop](drill-wood-chop.md) — Wood chop — diagonal cable rotational core exercise targeting obliques and transverse abdominis; four angle variations (high-to-low, low-to-high, horizontal, kneeling) for basketball rotational power.
- [Drill flex shooting two players](drill-flex-shooting-two-players.md) — Flex offense shooting drill for 2 players off vertical/back screens — alternating roles, coach passers, self-rebound and switch lines [S7, p.143].
- [Drill flex shooting three players](drill-flex-shooting-three-players.md) — Flex offense shooting drill for 3 players (5, 2, 3) with two balls and two coach passers — vertical screen or back screen read with roll option [S7, p.144].
- [Drill flex shooting two screens](drill-flex-shooting-two-screens.md) — Flex offense 4-on-4 shooting drill with two simultaneous screens — cutter reads slide-through (fade) or trail (curl), screeners roll to basket [S7, pp.144-145].
- [Drill flex screen the screener shooting](drill-flex-screen-the-screener-shooting.md) — Flex offense 4-on-4 screen-the-screener shooting drill with skip pass continuity — back screen for 2, high screen for 4, skip pass, repeat both sides [S7, pp.145].
- [Drill zigzag on ball pressure](drill-zigzag-on-ball-pressure.md) — Four-phase zigzag on-the-ball pressure drill: baseline-to-half-court dribble containment, ball-jamming on pick-up, and live 1-on-1 dribble cutting — Mike Fratello [S7].
- [Drill five second jamming](drill-five-second-jamming.md) — Five-second jamming drill: defender guards two hard dribbles then jams the ball (crossed wrists) every time the offensive player picks it up — Mike Fratello [S7].
- [Drill fratello closeout baseline](drill-fratello-closeout-baseline.md) — Mike Fratello's closeout drill: defender recovers from the paint, closes out with the chest (not hands) to cut off the baseline drive on alternating wing passes [S7].
- [Drill fratello 2v2 help recover](drill-fratello-2v2-help-recover.md) — Fratello 2-on-2 help-and-recover drill: X1 covers ball on the wing, X2 helps and recovers on baseline drive while 2 slides to corner — communication is the key [S7].
- [Drill fratello 3v3 help recover](drill-fratello-3v3-help-recover.md) — Fratello 3-on-3 help-and-recover / full-rotation drill: baseline drives and middle penetration trigger wing rotations and full-rotation trapping — live until score or stop [S7].
- [Drill obrien press 1v1](drill-obrien-press-1v1.md) — O'Brien full-court press 1-on-1 drill: half-court sideline, deny inbounds, pressure into speed dribble, back-tip if beaten — simultaneous at both ends [S7].
- [Drill obrien press 2v2](drill-obrien-press-2v2.md) — O'Brien full-court press 2-on-2 drill: half-court sideline, white or black press alignment, live after inbounds — deny, force speed dribble, trap, back-tip [S7].
- [Drill obrien press 3v3](drill-obrien-press-3v3.md) — O'Brien full-court press 3-on-3 drill: full court, white or black press alignment, live until ball is dead — key drill for reading press-offense alignments and building denial aggressiveness [S7].
- [Drill obrien press 4v4v4](drill-obrien-press-4v4v4.md) — O'Brien 4-4-4 press drill: three teams of four cycle through offense, defense, and tandem/half-court defense — simultaneous press and fast-break training on a full court [S7].
- [Drill circle pass warmup](drill-circle-pass-warmup.md) — Circle pass warm-up drill: 5 players inside/outside 3PT arc pass simultaneously and sprint to exchange positions — builds passing timing, conditioning, and court awareness [S7].
- [Drill flex elbow shooting](drill-flex-elbow-shooting.md) — Flex elbow shooting drill: single player fakes low, cuts high to each elbow alternately, receives from coach, and shoots — building game-realistic elbow jump shots with precision cuts [S7].
- [Drill chair series eastman](drill-chair-series-eastman.md) — Kevin Eastman's complete chair drill series: Intensity Layup, Elbow Jump Shot, Reverse Elbow Pick-Up, Four Chairs, Pin-Down Pull-Up, Dribble Intos, Cut Intos, Figure-8 Shooting, Flare Screen Shooting — all using chairs with balls to simulate low catches and game-speed scoring [S7].
- [Drill run the line](drill-run-the-line.md) — Run the Line drill: player catches and shoots from one elbow, sprints to the other, catches and shoots — continuous elbow-to-elbow jump shot conditioning drill [S7].
- [Drill 1on1 baseline touch](drill-1on1-baseline-touch.md) — 1-on-1 Baseline Touch drills: two players sprint to baseline and cut to wing (or inside the lane for bigs), first one out gets the ball — live 1-on-1 scoring drill off a competitive sprint [S7].
- [Drill 1on1 half court attack](drill-1on1-half-court-attack.md) — 1-on-1 Half-Court Attack drill: offensive player curls around a chair near mid-court, dribbles to the rim; defender races around the other chair to cut them off — live 1-on-1 from half court [S7].
- [Drill x with ball tossed ahead](drill-x-with-ball-tossed-ahead.md) — Basketball-specific warm-up drill combining defensive slides (X pattern), sprint, and chase-the-ball layup — develops defensive footwork, closeout mechanics, and transition acceleration in one continuous sequence.
- [Drill three line lateral footwork](drill-three-line-lateral-footwork.md) — Three-line lateral movement drill: both feet in each space between three taped lines on the court — builds foot-mind coordination, lateral quickness, and proper non-crossover footwork at maximum speed.
- [Drill line slide change direction](drill-line-slide-change-direction.md) — Line slide with change of direction: lateral defensive slides through taped lines with 45-degree angled lines requiring a pivot and direction reversal — builds defensive slide technique and change-of-direction ability.
- [Drill weak side help conditioning](drill-weak-side-help-conditioning.md) — Dalatri's weak-side help conditioning drill: defender starts on the weak side, sprints to close out, forces a pass to the top, then closes out again and contains penetration — combines conditioning with live defensive decision-making.
- [Drill sprint catch shoot conditioning](drill-sprint-catch-shoot-conditioning.md) — Sprint-catch-shoot conditioning drill: full-court baseline-to-baseline sprints with catch-and-shoot, pull-up dribble, and drive-to-layup sequences — combines cardiovascular conditioning with offensive skill execution under fatigue.
- [Drill offense transition defense sequence](drill-offense-transition-defense-sequence.md) — Offense-Transition-Defense conditioning sequence: full-court loop combining offense (catch-and-shoot), defensive movement (lane slides or help-and-recover), and transition between them — simulates game conditioning demands.
- [Drill flex offense two player shooting](drill-flex-offense-two-player-shooting.md) — 2-player flex shooting drill: players cut off vertical screens (over or under) using two coach-passers — practice off-screen reads in the flex offense.
- [Drill flex offense three player shooting](drill-flex-offense-three-player-shooting.md) — 3-player flex shooting drill with two balls and coach passers — adds the post roll as a third passing/scoring option off the screen-the-screener action.
- [Drill flex offense back screen shooting](drill-flex-offense-back-screen-shooting.md) — Flex back-screen shooting drill: 3 uses 2's screen to back-screen for 5, creating three simultaneous scoring options off one action.
- [Drill flex offense two screen shooting](drill-flex-offense-two-screen-shooting.md) — 4-on-4 flex drill: shooter reads two simultaneous screens and chooses which to use — fade, curl, or screener roll — based on defender movement.
- [Drill flex offense screen the screener drill](drill-flex-offense-screen-the-screener-drill.md) — 4-on-4 flex screen-the-screener drill: back screen triggers immediate screen-the-screener, then continues on both sides of the floor — Magnano's core flex teaching drill.
- [Drill three line fast break](drill-three-line-fast-break.md) — Karl/Moe three-line full-court fast-break drill: wings sprint sidelines, PG pushes on dribble, players free to cut/give-and-go; 10–15 minutes, no defense.
- [Drill five player passing game fast break](drill-five-player-passing-game-fast-break.md) — Karl/Moe five-player passing game fast-break drill: full-speed unrestricted passing game until a player calls timeout from exhaustion — builds conditioning and decision-making simultaneously.
- [Drill beep beep fast break](drill-beep-beep-fast-break.md) — Karl/Moe 'Beep-Beep' 5-on-5 drill: PG must push and shoot or make one pass for an immediate shot, then defense transitions to offense — trains fast-break pace and conditioning simultaneously.
- [Drill double drag dantoni](drill-double-drag-dantoni.md) — D'Antoni Double Drag drill: two big men set a stagger screen for a coach/ball handler — one rolls to basket, one pops outside — training the secondary break's most common two-trailer action.
- [Drill dribble drags dantoni](drill-dribble-drags-dantoni.md) — D'Antoni Dribble Drags drill: ball handler dribbles toward a cutting teammate for a hand-off, player sets a side screen and rolls to basket — trains secondary break dribble hand-off and screen-roll timing.
- [Drill rim runs dantoni](drill-rim-runs-dantoni.md) — D'Antoni Rim Runs drill: coach dribbles baseline, player sets a side screen and rolls opposite for a lob layup/dunk; variation: cutter goes to short corner for jump shot — trains secondary break side-screen and roll.
- [Drill read defense step up dantoni](drill-read-defense-step-up-dantoni.md) — D'Antoni 'Read the Defense: Step Up' drill — when defense forces ball handler sideline, player follows, screens, and rolls baseline for a layup — training the step-up counter to sideline pressure.
- [Drill pinch post series dantoni](drill-pinch-post-series-dantoni.md) — D'Antoni Pinch Post Series: big men catch at the elbow corners, read a cutting coach-as-defender, and choose to drive to basket, shoot a face-up jumper, or execute a hand-off screen-roll — three finishes in one drill.
- [Drill zigzag on ball press](drill-zigzag-on-ball-press.md) — Mike Fratello's 4-part zigzag full-court on-ball pressure drill — step-and-slide to cut off lane and sideline, building up to live 1-on-1 to half-court.
- [Drill five second on ball](drill-five-second-on-ball.md) — Five-Second Drill: defender steps-slides to guard two hard dribbles then jams the ball overhead with crossed wrists — Mike Fratello's inbounds-line pressure drill.
- [Drill fratello closeout drive](drill-fratello-closeout-drive.md) — Fratello's closeout drill: single defender in the lane must close out and chest-cut baseline drivers on alternating wing passes from a coach — no hands, body contact only.
- [Drill help and recover 3v3](drill-help-and-recover-3v3.md) — Fratello's 3-on-3 help-and-recover drill: full baseline rotation and two middle-penetration coverage options (help-and-recover and full rotation) — live until scored or possession secured.
- [Drill 4 4 4 full court press](drill-4-4-4-full-court-press.md) — The 4-4-4 full-court press drill (Jim O'Brien): three teams of four cycling offense → defense → rest in a continuous full-court live drill that teaches press execution and transition simultaneously.
- [Drill press 1v1 inbounds](drill-press-1v1-inbounds.md) — O'Brien's 1-on-1 full-court press drill: deny the inbounds pass on one half of the court, then pressure the dribbler into a speed dribble and practice back-tipping from behind.
- [Drill press 2v2 inbounds](drill-press-2v2-inbounds.md) — O'Brien's 2-on-2 full-court press drill: deny the inbounds pass (White and Black variants), force the speed dribble and trap, with back-tip recovery if the trap is broken.
- [Drill drive and kick series](drill-drive-and-kick-series.md) — the head coach's Drive-and-Kick Series (3-out, 2-in): five variations of the middle and baseline drive with all read-based kick-out options — core pro offensive drill.
- [Drill closeout 1 2](drill-closeout-1-2.md) — the head coach's Closeout 1 and Closeout 2 defensive movement drills — sprint-close-out with no middle, medicine ball slides — building defensive stance and lateral quickness.
- [Drill shell shooting frank](drill-shell-shooting-frank.md) — the head coach's Shell Shooting format: 3 teams of 4 rotate offense/defense/shooting simultaneously, eliminating dead time — learned from the originating head coach.
- [Drill green post defense](drill-green-post-defense.md) — The 'Green' drill: 4-on-4 shell drill teaching fronting the low post (Green = front), weak-side tag, ball pressure, elbow protection, and help positioning when the guard slice-cuts to post.
- [Drill five on four scramble](drill-five-on-four-scramble.md) — Five-on-Four Scramble drill: 4 defenders in a diamond vs 5 offensive players (5 passes, 3 dribbles limit) — defense earns its fifth man when they get a stop or after a score.
- [Drill five on five change](drill-five-on-five-change.md) — Five-on-Five Change drill: coach yells 'Change!' — offense drops ball, sprints to defense; new offense throws ahead to a coach and attacks; trains both O-to-D and D-to-O transitions.
- [Drill help and recover 2v2](drill-help-and-recover-2v2.md) — the head coach's two-on-two help-and-recover drills (baseline drive version and middle drive version): teach the help-and-recover principle off dribble penetration in two scenarios.
- [Drill 55 second shooting frank](drill-55-second-shooting-frank.md) — the head coach's 55-second shooting drill: shooter attacks the wing then fades to corner in 55-second bursts with passer (2 balls) and rebounder rotating every 5 seconds.
- [Drill circle pass](drill-circle-pass.md) — Circle Pass warm-up drill: 5 players inside/outside the 3PT arc pass simultaneously and sprint to exchange positions — builds passing timing, sprint conditioning, and spatial awareness.
- [Drill reverse replace drive](drill-reverse-replace-drive.md) — Reverse, Replace, and Drive warm-up drill: pass → follow → replace sequence teaches passing off movement, cutting, and driving to the basket in a continuous flow.
- [Drill over and under](drill-over-and-under.md) — Over and Under drill: two players sprint to exchange positions (corner and wing), receive coach passes, and shoot jump shots — simulates game-speed positional reads.
- [Drill eastman flex elbow](drill-eastman-flex-elbow.md) — Eastman Flex Elbow drill: player fakes a cut, comes high to the elbow, receives from coach, and shoots — both elbows, set reps; sharpens flex cut timing and elbow jump shot mechanics.
- [Drill eastman chair shooting series](drill-eastman-chair-shooting-series.md) — Kevin Eastman's complete pro chair shooting drill series (6 drills): intensity layup, elbow jump shot, reverse elbow pick-up, four chairs, figure-8 shooting, and flare screen shooting — using chairs with balls to simulate low-catch game reads.
- [Drill quick square ups](drill-quick-square-ups.md) — Quick Square-Ups drill: coach yells 'Right' or 'Left' mid-air; player pivots, squares on the called foot, and shoots — builds reactive pivot footwork for catch-and-shoot decisions.
- [Drill eastman 1on1 baseline touch](drill-eastman-1on1-baseline-touch.md) — One-on-One Baseline Touch drill (perimeter and bigs versions): two players sprint to the baseline, cut back to their spot, and compete 1-on-1 — the first player out receives the ball.
- [Drill eastman 1on1 halfcourt attack](drill-eastman-1on1-halfcourt-attack.md) — One-on-One Half-Court Attack: offensive player curls around a mid-court chair and attacks the rim while defender runs a parallel path to beat the offense to the inside — competitive 1-on-1.
- [Drill dribble intos](drill-dribble-intos.md) — Dribble Intos drill: player dribbles full speed into a triangle of chairs at the free-throw line and pulls up for a two-count stop jump shot — builds pull-up discipline and deceleration control.
- [Drill cut intos](drill-cut-intos.md) — Cut Intos drill: player fakes a basket cut, cuts into a grouping of chairs at the elbow, receives a pass, makes a two-count stop, and shoots — simulates receiving under game-like traffic conditions.
- [Drill pin down pull up](drill-pin-down-pull-up.md) — Pin Down Pull Up drill: player fakes inside, sprints to a wing chair, squares and shoots, sprints to mid-court, then repeats to the other side — high-rep conditioning and catch-and-shoot training.
- [Drill straight hop s9](drill-straight-hop-s9.md) — Step 1 of the S9 Power Jump Chain: straight hop — ankle-dominant explosive hop building elastic rebound, take-off/landing patterns, and joint preparation for harder jump work.
- [Drill squat jump s9](drill-squat-jump-s9.md) — Step 2 of the S9 Power Jump Chain: squat jump — integrates knee and hip joints into the jump pattern, the cornerstone of all jumping techniques.
- [Drill vertical leap s9](drill-vertical-leap-s9.md) — Step 3 of the S9 Power Jump Chain: vertical leap — adds explosive arm swing to the squat jump, developing total upper/lower body coordination for maximum jump height.
- [Drill block jump s9](drill-block-jump-s9.md) — Step 4 of the S9 Power Jump Chain: block jump — converts horizontal running momentum into vertical jump height, an essential skill for fast-break finishes and advanced acrobatics.
- [Drill butt kick jump s9](drill-butt-kick-jump-s9.md) — Step 5 of the S9 Power Jump Chain: butt-kick jump — first tuck-chain drill developing hip flexor conditioning, leg speed, and the objective performance criteria of mid-air heel-to-glute contact.
- [Drill incline pop up](drill-incline-pop-up.md) — Step 1 of the Power Pushup Chain: explosive incline pop-up off a chest-height surface — the safest entry point for developing upper-body plyometric pushing power. [S9]
- [Drill kneeling push off](drill-kneeling-push-off.md) — Step 2 of the Power Pushup Chain: explosive kneeling push-off — a significant power jump that reveals whether athletes can convert strength into speed. [S9]
- [Drill flat pop up](drill-flat-pop-up.md) — Step 3 of the Power Pushup Chain: flat floor pop-up — the foundational explosive pushup that builds airtime for all harder plyometric variations. [S9]
- [Drill clap pushup](drill-clap-pushup.md) — Step 4 of the Power Pushup Chain: clap pushup — the classic upper-body explosive exercise building torso power, quick hands, and shoulder toughness. [S9]
- [Drill chest strike pushup](drill-chest-strike-pushup.md) — Step 5 of the Power Pushup Chain: chest-strike pushup — hands whip upward to slap the chest in mid-air, requiring greater airtime and bicep fast-twitch activation than clap pushups. [S9]
- [Drill hip strike pushup](drill-hip-strike-pushup.md) — Step 6 of the Power Pushup Chain: hip-strike pushup — hands whip back to slap the hips in mid-air, bridging between front-body and behind-the-back explosive pushup work. [S9]
- [Drill convict pushup](drill-convict-pushup.md) — Step 7 of the Power Pushup Chain: convict pushup (behind-the-back clap) — hands whip back and clap together behind the spine in mid-air, requiring extreme upper-body explosive power. [S9]
- [Drill half super pushup](drill-half-super-pushup.md) — Step 8 of the Power Pushup Chain: half-super pushup — both hands thrust forward beyond the head in mid-air, training extreme shoulder speed as the upper-body component of the Superman. [S9]
- [Drill full body pop up pushup](drill-full-body-pop-up-pushup.md) — Step 9 of the Power Pushup Chain: full body pop-up — all four limbs leave the floor simultaneously, training total-body explosive power as the prerequisite for the Superman pushup. [S9]
- [Drill push getup](drill-push-getup.md) — Push Get-Up small-space drill — explode from push-up position into standing; upper-lower body integration drill and prerequisite for Aztec push-ups.
- [Drill kip up chain](drill-kip-up-chain.md) — The complete 10-step kip-up progressive chain from rolling sit-up through no-hands kip-up — builds hip snap, floor-to-feet explosiveness, and core power.
- [Drill bridge kip](drill-bridge-kip.md) — Bridge kip (Step 4 of kip-up chain): roll to upper-back, explode legs in arc + push palms to lift head/upper-back off floor — builds lower-body power for the full kip-up.
- [Drill butt kip](drill-butt-kip.md) — Butt kip (Step 5 of kip-up chain): first kip variation where palms leave the floor and the torso is thrown forward to land on both butt and feet with an upright torso.
- [Drill half kip](drill-half-kip.md) — Half kip (Step 6 of kip-up chain): fuses the leg-arc and torso-throw to land on both feet for a fraction of a second before sitting back — the critical momentum threshold step.
- [Drill kip up](drill-kip-up.md) — The classic kip-up (Step 7): explosive floor-to-standing movement demanding an explosive waist, fast legs, and total-body agility — the marquee step of the kip-up chain.
- [Drill straight leg kip up](drill-straight-leg-kip-up.md) — Straight-leg kip-up (Step 8): advanced kip-up variant starting with legs straight — eliminates thigh/glute contribution and forces hips/waist to generate all momentum.
- [Drill wushu kip up](drill-wushu-kip-up.md) — Wushu kip-up (Step 9): arms extended at right-angles to body (not in bridge position) — systematically reduces arm contribution to force hip/waist to drive the movement toward hands-free kip-up.
- [Drill no hands kip up](drill-no-hands-kip-up.md) — No-hands kip-up (Master Step): the ultimate floor-to-standing explosive movement with arms never touching the floor — powered entirely by waist and leg drive.
- [Drill kip up small space variations](drill-kip-up-small-space-variations.md) — S9 small-space kip-up ancillary drills: bridge push-offs (wall), sitting kips (kneeling), and prone kip (face-down) — equipment-free speed/power supplements to the kip-up chain.
- [Drill front flip chain](drill-front-flip-chain.md) — The complete 10-step front flip progressive chain from S9 Ch.7: shoulder roll → press roll → jump roll → handstand roll → back-drop handspring → front handspring → flyspring → back-drop flip → running front flip → standing front flip.
- [Drill shoulder roll s9](drill-shoulder-roll-s9.md) — Step 1 of the front flip chain: the shoulder roll (ukemi/breakfall) — safest forward roll, loading the upper-back and protecting wrists/elbows/shoulders while conditioning the athlete to forward rotation.
- [Drill press roll s9](drill-press-roll-s9.md) — Step 2 of the front flip chain: the press roll — bilateral palm-braced forward roll that begins training the hands as load-bearing levers, progressively conditioning the upper limbs for handspring forces.
- [Drill jump roll s9](drill-jump-roll-s9.md) — Step 3 of the front flip chain: the jump roll — introduces upward explosive power by jumping UP before hands contact the floor, training the brain to tolerate rotation while building the plyometric arm-catch demand.
- [Drill handstand roll s9](drill-handstand-roll-s9.md) — Step 4 of the front flip chain: the handstand roll — combines explosive leg kick-up to momentary handstand with a forward roll, the final roll in the chain and the gateway to back-drop handsprings.
- [Drill backdrop handspring s9](drill-backdrop-handspring-s9.md) — Step 5 of the front flip chain: the back-drop handspring — running front handspring with an incomplete rotation, landing feet-then-glutes; the bridge from rolls to full handsprings requiring minimal upper-body strength.
- [Drill front handspring s9](drill-front-handspring-s9.md) — Step 6 of the front flip chain: the front handspring — full running front handspring landing on both feet; a key athleticism benchmark demonstrating running, blocking, jumping, explosive pressing, rotational tolerance, and landing mastery.
- [Drill flyspring s9](drill-flyspring-s9.md) — Step 7 of the front flip chain: the flyspring (bounder) — symmetrical front handspring with a bilateral two-foot block jump requiring significantly more total-body power; the bridge to the true front flip.
- [Drill backdrop flip s9](drill-backdrop-flip-s9.md) — Step 8 of the front flip chain: the back-drop flip — a true no-hands front flip rotation with an incomplete landing (feet then glutes); the 'missing link' drill requiring maximum padding and building rotation power for the running front flip.
- [Drill back flip master](drill-back-flip-master.md) — The back flip master step (Step 10 of back flip chain): vertical jump + tuck at peak height creates full backward rotation without hand contact — the pinnacle of the explosive calisthenics back-flip series.
- [Drill dip progression chain](drill-dip-progression-chain.md) — 10-step dip progression chain from Explosive Calisthenics — bent dips through horizontal bar dips — building the pressing strength required for the muscle-up's dip-press, plus explosive dip variations.
- [Drill explosive dip variations](drill-explosive-dip-variations.md) — Explosive dip variations from Explosive Calisthenics — walking dips, hopping dips, clap dips, 180 power dips, and swing dips — for building upper-body speed-strength and reactive pressing power on the parallel bars.
- [Drill muscle up variations](drill-muscle-up-variations.md) — Advanced muscle-up variations from S9: swing dips, underhand muscle-up, archer muscle-up, and full kip — building total-body power, grip strength, and asymmetric pulling ability.
- [Drill small space calisthenics](drill-small-space-calisthenics.md) — Three no-equipment small-space power drills from S9: sideways pop-ups (lateral push-up power), pike slaps (explosive abdominal/total-body), and jump kicks (unilateral hip power) — usable as warm-ups or finishers.
- [Drill basketball wall reaction drills](drill-basketball-wall-reaction-drills.md) — Three solo basketball wall drills (Jump Throw, 360 Throw, Dip Throw) building reflexes, reaction time, and explosive movement with only a wall and a basketball — from S9.
- [Drill animal agility drills s9](drill-animal-agility-drills-s9.md) — Ten animal agility drills from S9 (bear walk, panther stalk, crocodile, dog sprint, locust jumps, crab walk, duck walk, kangaroo hop, chimp swing, bat flips, monkey turns) — asymmetrical movement building lateral chain, trunk stability, and coordination.
- [Drill straight hop explosive](drill-straight-hop-explosive.md) — Step 1 of the S9 Power Jump Chain — ankle-driven straight hop with minimal knee bend; foundational jump drill teaching take-off patterns, landing mechanics, and elastic ankle rebound.
- [Drill squat jump explosive](drill-squat-jump-explosive.md) — Step 2 of the S9 Power Jump Chain — full knee-bend squat jump; cornerstone jumping drill that adds hip and knee power to the ankle spring built in Step 1.
- [Drill vertical leap explosive](drill-vertical-leap-explosive.md) — Step 3 of the S9 Power Jump Chain — vertical leap with full arm swing; coordinates upper and lower body for maximum jump height and momentum, measurable via Sargent Jump Test.
- [Drill block jump](drill-block-jump.md) — Step 4 of the S9 Power Jump Chain — run-up block jump converting horizontal momentum into vertical height; essential skill for fast-break finishes and prerequisite for front flips.
- [Drill butt kick jump](drill-butt-kick-jump.md) — Step 5 of the S9 Power Jump Chain — squat jump with heel-to-glute kick at peak height; first hip flexor conditioning drill and first step with objective performance criteria in the chain.
- [Drill slap tuck jump](drill-slap-tuck-jump.md) — Slap tuck jump (Step 6 of jump chain) — squat-jump with knees driven to hip level to slap hands at peak; intermediate step toward full tuck jump [S9].
- [Drill tuck jump s9](drill-tuck-jump-s9.md) — Tuck jump (Step 7 of jump chain) — explosive bilateral jump drawing knees to chest at peak height; essential skill for lower-body power and advanced acrobatics [S9].
- [Drill catch tuck jump](drill-catch-tuck-jump.md) — Catch tuck jump (Step 8 of jump chain) — tuck jump with arms pulling shins into chest at peak, building trunk compression power for advanced acrobatics [S9].
- [Drill thread jump](drill-thread-jump.md) — Thread jump (Step 9 of jump chain) — unilateral jump threading the free foot through the hand-foot gap; builds one-leg tuck power for suicide jumps [S9].
- [Drill suicide jump](drill-suicide-jump.md) — Suicide jump (Master Step of jump chain) — tuck jump threading a held bar/dowel under both feet in mid-air; the ultimate explosive tuck drill [S9].
- [Drill cossacks small space](drill-cossacks-small-space.md) — Cossacks small-space drill — low-stance alternating leg extensions building lower-body supple strength, power in a stretched range, and balance [S9].
- [Drill wide to close popups](drill-wide-to-close-popups.md) — Wide-to-Close Pop-Ups (Small Space Drill) — explosive push-up hand-spread in mid-air training total upper-body power by pairing fast arms with fast legs [S9].
- [Drill wall threads](drill-wall-threads.md) — Wall Threads (Small Space Drill) — one foot on a vertical surface, jump over it keeping foot in place; builds fast feet and threading coordination for jump chain work [S9].
- [Drill superman pushup](drill-superman-pushup.md) — Superman pushup — master-level explosive bodyweight exercise: full-body airborne push-up with hands thrust forward and legs kicked back simultaneously, training anterior/posterior chain and upper-body power.
- [Drill push get up](drill-push-get-up.md) — Push Get-Up — explosive small-space drill: from pushup position, dip and explode up, bringing legs in to finish standing — upper-lower body integration and Aztec pushup prerequisite.
- [Drill round the clock pushups](drill-round-the-clock-pushups.md) — Round-the-Clock Pushups — explosive endurance small-space drill: rhythmic lateral plyometric pushups rotating 360° around a fixed foot pivot point, building upper-body explosive endurance.
- [Drill 360 jump](drill-360-jump.md) — 360 Jump — small-space rotational jump drill: jump and spin a full 360° landing back in place, building lower-body power, rotational body control, and bilateral coordination.
- [Drill rolling sit up](drill-rolling-sit-up.md) — Rolling Sit-Up (Kip-Up Chain Step 1) — floor conditioning drill: roll back with knees to head and forward to seated, building midsection/hip power and kip-up movement patterns.
- [Drill rolling squat](drill-rolling-squat.md) — Rolling Squat (Kip-Up Chain Step 2) — floor-to-standing momentum drill: roll back, then generate enough forward momentum to stand from a squat — the key forward-momentum skill for the kip-up.
- [Drill shoulder pop](drill-shoulder-pop.md) — Shoulder Pop (Kip-Up Chain Step 3) — wrist/shoulder conditioning drill: explosive vertical leg kick from the roll-up position with a simultaneous palm push that briefly lifts shoulders off the floor.
- [Drill kip up progression chain](drill-kip-up-progression-chain.md) — Complete 7-step kip-up progression chain (bridge kip → no-hands kip-up) — total-body explosive floor-to-standing movement building hip power, waist speed, and agility [S9].
- [Drill kip up small space drills](drill-kip-up-small-space-drills.md) — Kip-up ancillary small-space drills (bridge push-offs, sitting kips, prone kip) — solo bodyweight speed/power tools for warming up or supplementing the kip-up chain [S9].
- [Drill shoulder roll front flip](drill-shoulder-roll-front-flip.md) — Shoulder Roll (Step 1 of front flip chain) — easiest forward rotation drill, joint-protective breakfall mechanics used in Japanese martial arts, builds rotation tolerance from scratch.
- [Drill press roll front flip](drill-press-roll-front-flip.md) — Press Roll (Step 2 of front flip chain) — both-palm guided forward roll building hand leverage and introducing arm-controlled rotation as preparation for handsprings.
- [Drill jump roll front flip](drill-jump-roll-front-flip.md) — Jump Roll (Step 3 of front flip chain) — explosive jump into a forward roll, building plyometric upper-body catching strength and kinesthetic rotation comfort.
- [Drill handstand roll front flip](drill-handstand-roll-front-flip.md) — Handstand Roll (Step 4 of front flip chain) — final roll in the chain; explosive leg kick to handstand position before rolling through, building arm strength for handsprings.
- [Drill back drop handspring](drill-back-drop-handspring.md) — Back-Drop Handspring (Step 5 of front flip chain) — partial handspring landing on feet and glutes; teaches the first portion of the handspring spin-out, accessible to even weak athletes.
- [Drill front handspring](drill-front-handspring.md) — Front Handspring (Step 6 of front flip chain) — full run-and-block handspring landing on both feet; builds running, blocking, jumping, explosive pressing, rotational tolerance, and landing as an explosive drill in its own right.
- [Drill flyspring](drill-flyspring.md) — Flyspring / Bounder (Step 7 of front flip chain) — symmetrical bilateral handspring (block jump off both feet, land on both feet) requiring much more total-body power than the front handspring.
- [Drill back drop flip](drill-back-drop-flip.md) — Back-Drop Flip (Step 8 of front flip chain) — first true airborne forward flip with a padded landing; the 'missing link' between flyspring and running front flip, always requiring maximum padding.
- [Drill running front flip](drill-running-front-flip.md) — Running front flip (Step 9 of front flip chain): block jump run-up, hand throw, knee tuck, and landing mechanics — easier than standing due to forward momentum.
- [Drill standing front flip](drill-standing-front-flip.md) — Master Step of the front flip chain: standing two-foot bilateral takeoff with simultaneous arm throw and knee tuck — the supreme explosive athleticism calisthenics benchmark.
- [Drill kojaks](drill-kojaks.md) — Kojaks small-space explosive pressing drill: pike position head-to-floor push-up with explosive hand-slap — builds pressing power for front handsprings.
- [Drill thrusters calisthenics](drill-thrusters-calisthenics.md) — Thrusters (burpees): prone knee tuck/extend in push-up position — small-space explosive hip flexor drill with high-rep cardio benefit for basketball conditioning.
- [Drill unilateral jump calisthenics](drill-unilateral-jump-calisthenics.md) — Unilateral jump (pistol squat jump): single-leg squat into a vertical jump — develops coordination, landing balance, ankle strength, and single-leg explosive power.
- [Drill rear shoulder roll](drill-rear-shoulder-roll.md) — Rear shoulder roll (Step 1 of back flip chain): low-impact backward roll over the shoulder protecting the neck — the foundational vestibular adaptation drill for rear rotation.
- [Drill rear press roll](drill-rear-press-roll.md) — Rear press roll (Step 2 of back flip chain): backward roll with hands bracing beside the head and pushing through the arms — progressive upper limb loading for backward rotation.
- [Drill bridge kick over](drill-bridge-kick-over.md) — Bridge kick-over (Step 3 of back flip chain) — from a full bridge, press foot against a wall to flip legs over the hands to standing; builds shoulder tolerance and vestibular comfort for backward rotation [S9].
- [Drill side macaco](drill-side-macaco.md) — Side macaco capoeira-derived drill (Step 4 of back flip chain) — squat-lean, one-palm pivot, swing legs around the side of the head; builds rotational shoulder mechanics and momentum for the back handspring [S9].
- [Drill back macaco](drill-back-macaco.md) — Back macaco (Step 5 of back flip chain) — evolution of side macaco where legs swing directly over the head; body briefly supported on one arm while inverted; builds the mechanics and height for the back handspring [S9].
- [Drill monkey flip](drill-monkey-flip.md) — Monkey flip (Step 6 of back flip chain) — standing entry where the pivot palm drops to the floor as feet leave it; the standing-start equivalent of the macaco and the ultimate one-handed flip preparation [S9].
- [Drill back handspring](drill-back-handspring.md) — Back handspring (Step 7 of back flip chain) — explosive diagonal backward jump landing on both locked arms then whipping feet to ground; the full two-handed backward flip that bridges macaco work to the back flip [S9].
- [Drill one arm back handspring](drill-one-arm-back-handspring.md) — One-arm back handspring (Step 8 of back flip chain) — back handspring with only one arm touching the floor as a brief pivot, forcing leg-power independence as transition toward the no-hands back flip [S9].
- [Drill four point back flip](drill-four-point-back-flip.md) — Four-point back flip (Step 9 of back flip chain) — transitional drill where hands and feet contact the ground simultaneously; bridges the back handspring to the no-hands back flip by developing maximum jump height and leg-whip speed [S9].
- [Drill back flip](drill-back-flip.md) — Back flip — Master Step of the back flip chain: vertical jump, peak-height tuck, arm pull, leg whip to land — no hands touch the floor; the pinnacle explosive calisthenics achievement requiring quick jump, massive hip snap, and total-body power [S9].
- [Drill swing kip](drill-swing-kip.md) — Swing Kip — Step 1 of the muscle-up chain: forward-rebound-backswing cycle on a bar that builds the momentum and hollow-body position essential for all explosive bar work.
- [Drill jumping pullup](drill-jumping-pullup.md) — Jumping Pullup — Step 2 of the muscle-up chain: use leg drive from a low bar to practice the diagonal back-and-in kipping pull arc, training explosive upper-body neurological patterns.
- [Drill kipping pullup](drill-kipping-pullup.md) — Kipping Pullup — Step 3 of the muscle-up chain: combine the swing kip and jumping pullup into one explosive bar movement, the cornerstone of all power bar training.
- [Drill pullup hop](drill-pullup-hop.md) — Pullup Hop — Step 4 of the muscle-up chain: at the top of a kipping pullup, briefly release hands from the bar to develop bar airtime, the precursor to the clap pullup.
- [Drill one arm wall push away](drill-one-arm-wall-push-away.md) — One-Arm Wall Push-Away — unilateral explosive wall push-up that builds powerful, bulletproof elbows; progressively harder by stepping feet further back from the wall.
- [Drill donkey kick](drill-donkey-kick.md) — Donkey Kick — explosive spine and posterior chain drill from a quadruped position: jump legs up and straighten in mid-air; warm-up for back handsprings and powerful spinal firing.
- [Drill scissors jump](drill-scissors-jump.md) — Scissors Jump — explosive alternating lunge jump with mid-air leg switch; builds vertical power, rapid hip movement, and trunk rotation for athletic performance.
- [Drill clap pullup](drill-clap-pullup.md) — Clap pullup — explosive calisthenics bar drill: swing kip to peak, release bar, clap hands, re-grip — step 5 in the muscle-up progression chain.
- [Drill chest pullup](drill-chest-pullup.md) — Chest pullup — advanced kipping pullup variant where the athlete pulls elbows behind the body to touch the chest to the bar; step 6 in the muscle-up chain.
- [Drill hip pullup](drill-hip-pullup.md) — Hip pullup — kipping bar drill where glute/posterior-chain thrust drives the hips to the bar; step 7 in the muscle-up chain and the gateway to the pull-over.
- [Drill jumping pullover](drill-jumping-pullover.md) — Jumping pullover — leg-assisted bar drill that teaches the pull-over technique for the muscle-up before doing it without support; step 8 in the muscle-up chain.
- [Drill bar pullover](drill-bar-pullover.md) — Bar pullover — full kipping pullover without leg assistance, pulling the torso over the bar and pausing in support position; step 9 and gateway to the muscle-up.
- [Drill muscle up](drill-muscle-up.md) — The muscle-up — the master calisthenics bar exercise combining a full kipping pullover with a dip-press to full arm extension above the bar; requires pull + push + power + timing.
- [Drill dip progressions](drill-dip-progressions.md) — 10-step dip progression chain from S9 — bent dips through horizontal bar dips — plus explosive variations (walking, hopping, clap, 180 power, swing dips) for muscle-up pressing strength.
- [Drill small space power drills](drill-small-space-power-drills.md) — Three no-equipment small-space explosive drills from S9 — Sideways Pop-Ups, Pike Slaps, and Jump Kick — usable as warm-ups, finishers, or ancillary power work.
- [Drill solo basketball reflex drills](drill-solo-basketball-reflex-drills.md) — Solo basketball reflex drills (Jump Throw, 360 Throw, Dip Throw) — individual wall/floor drills building whole-body reaction time, coordination, and explosive athleticism [S9].
- [Drill animal agility drills](drill-animal-agility-drills.md) — Ten animal agility drills (Bear Walk, Panther Stalk, Dog Sprint, Locust Jumps, Crab Walk, Duck Walk, Kangaroo Hop, Chimp Swing, Bat Flips, Monkey Turns) — quadrupedal and hanging calisthenics developing lateral chain, coordination, and joint resilience [S9].
- [Drill 55 second shooting format](drill-55-second-shooting-format.md) — The 55-second shooting drill format: three players rotate passer→shooter→rebounder every 55 seconds, integrating cutting, catching, pivoting, shooting, and outlet passing in 3-minute total sessions.
- [Drill shell drill rebounding](drill-shell-drill-rebounding.md) — Defensive shell drill used as a rebounding drill: perimeter ball movement followed by a live shot triggers defensive box-outs and offensive rebound escape attempts from all three distance scenarios.
- [Drill 3on2 to 2on1 transition](drill-3on2-to-2on1-transition.md) — 3-on-2 to 2-on-1 Transition Drill: two seated defenders scramble up and sprint back to defend a 3-on-2, with basket man / ball man communication; after a score or stop, two offensive players become a 2-on-1 going the other way.
- [Drill breakdown pivoting shooters](drill-breakdown-pivoting-shooters.md) — Circle-based breakdown footwork drills for shooters — 4 players per foul-line circle, clockwise and counterclockwise, cutting and dribbling versions — isolate inside-heel pivot and square-up without the distraction of actual shooting.
- [Drill mass footwork rotation](drill-mass-footwork-rotation.md) — Mass footwork rotation drill (S6): three 4-man groups work simultaneously on perimeter passing/driving and post scoring footwork, rotating every 55 seconds — covers all 4 spots in 4 minutes.
- [Drill daily pre practice routine s6](drill-daily-pre-practice-routine-s6.md) — 42-minute scoreboard-timed daily pre-practice routine for up to 24 players (varsity + JV) covering stretching, dribbling, shooting, pivoting, rebounding, and defensive fundamentals.
- [Drill timed shooting series](drill-timed-shooting-series.md) — Timed 2-player shooting drill series (inside, outside, 3PT zones) — 3 min per zone with benchmarked shot counts and accuracy targets at 50/60/70%.
- [Drill closeout shooting off pass](drill-closeout-shooting-off-pass.md) — Closeout shooting drill off the pass — passer follows pass and closes out on shooter; 2-player and rapid-fire 3-player variants with benchmarked accuracy targets.
- [Drill closeout shooting off dribble series](drill-closeout-shooting-off-dribble-series.md) — Progressive closeout shooting drill series off the dribble — shot fake into drive, pull-up, power layup, dish, penetrate-and-pitch, with benchmarked accuracy targets for 2–4 players.
- [Drill 55 second shooting drill](drill-55-second-shooting-drill.md) — Basic 55-second shooting drill (3-player groups) — 55 seconds per role (shooter/passer/rebounder), rotating through all three; competitive with individual and group goals and penalty for losers.
- [Drill power shots post bubble](drill-power-shots-post-bubble.md) — Post power shot drills with bubble defender — low-block drop step, show-and-go opposite, both sides, 2-minute timed segments; includes solo self-toss variation.
- [Drill pivot and pass station](drill-pivot-and-pass-station.md) — Three-station rotating drill training the pivot-and-pass technique: dribbler/passer, ball defender, and pass receiver/shooter — 55-second rotations, 6-minute total.
- [Drill circle box out](drill-circle-box-out.md) — Competitive 1-on-1 box-out drill using the center jump circle to teach all defensive box-out methods and all three offensive rebound escape techniques.
- [Drill shell rebounding](drill-shell-rebounding.md) — Shell drill variant used as an offensive/defensive rebounding drill: defense allows perimeter passes then a shot, players box out from shooter, one-pass-away, and help positions — all rotate offense/defense.
- [Drill super transition](drill-super-transition.md) — 15-player overload transition drill: Squad A plays offense/defense against Squad B in 5v5, then immediately defends a head-start fast break by Squad C — trains O-to-D and D-to-O transitions under maximum pressure.
- [Drill 3on2 to 2on1 transition s6](drill-3on2-to-2on1-transition-s6.md) — Comprehensive 3v2→2v1 transition drill from S6: defenders start seated, communicate basket/ball man roles, and defend while 3 offensive players run wide-lane fast break — multiple start variations included.
- [Drill pivot and pass](drill-pivot-and-pass.md) — Three-player pivot-and-pass drill: passer uses step-out/rip-through vs. live defender while receiver pivots on the catch and shoots; rotates every 55 seconds for 3 minutes covering all fundamentals.
- [Drill mass ballhandling pivoting](drill-mass-ballhandling-pivoting.md) — Full-team mass drill: initial passer pivots vs. two trappers, first pass receiver pivots and continues the sequence — building ballhandling, pivoting, trapping, and pass-reception skills across the whole court simultaneously.
- [Drill breakdown pivoting circle](drill-breakdown-pivoting-circle.md) — Circle breakdown pivoting drill for shooters — groups of 4 jog around court circles and pivot/square up on command, both clockwise and counterclockwise, training inside-heel footwork for cutters and dribblers.
- [Drill cutting outlet pass shooting](drill-cutting-outlet-pass-shooting.md) — Cutting, outlet pass, and shooting drill — pairs at each basket combine inside-heel pivot catch-and-shoot, rebounding technique, outlet passing pivots, and progressive shot-fake/dribble variations in a full-perimeter rotation.
- [Drill push push defensive](drill-push-push-defensive.md) — Push-Push mass defensive drill — coach-led simulation of dribble penetration teaches all four on-ball defensive foot movements (advance, drop-and-swing, push-off, slide) to the full squad simultaneously.
- [Drill push and talk defensive](drill-push-and-talk-defensive.md) — Push-and-Talk defensive maze drill — 5 defenders traverse a full-court course with 6 direction changes using the advance/drop-and-swing/push-off/slide sequence; staggered starts force communication.
- [Drill pride zigzag defensive](drill-pride-zigzag-defensive.md) — Zigzag Pride defensive drill — full-court live 1v1 in dribble alleys; defender must turn the dribbler 3+ times using proper footwork; hands-behind-back variation eliminates reaching fouls.
- [Drill mass footwork breakdown](drill-mass-footwork-breakdown.md) — Mass footwork breakdown drill — 12-player team split into 3 four-man groups working simultaneously; 55-second rotations cover all four roles (passer, cutter, post, defender) in 4 minutes.
- [Drill uphill acceleration run](drill-uphill-acceleration-run.md) — Uphill acceleration run (20–35° incline, 4–8 sec efforts) — resisted acceleration drill building starting power and stride length.
- [Drill heavy sled pulls](drill-heavy-sled-pulls.md) — Heavy sled pull resisted acceleration drill — drag a weighted sled 15–20 yards to enhance starting power and stride length.
- [Drill partner resisted starts](drill-partner-resisted-starts.md) — Partner-resisted starts — a partner uses hands or towel at the waist to resist the first 8–10 strides of acceleration, building starting power.
- [Drill partner tubing assisted acceleration](drill-partner-tubing-assisted-acceleration.md) — Partner tubing-assisted acceleration — rubber tubing pulled by a partner 15–25 yards ahead assists the runner's first steps, improving stride frequency.
- [Drill harness pull](drill-harness-pull.md) — Harness pull assisted acceleration — towed by a partner via a harness/handle system at half-speed to run faster than normal and improve acceleration.
- [Drill partner assisted let gos](drill-partner-assisted-let-gos.md) — Partner-assisted let-gos (contrast acceleration) — held at 45° lean by partner for 5 strides, then released to explode forward, teaching rapid speed transitions.
- [Drill bullet belt](drill-bullet-belt.md) — Bullet belt contrast acceleration — Velcro-release belt held by partner until enough force breaks the Velcro, teaching explosive acceleration transition.
- [Drill skip for height](drill-skip-for-height.md) — Skip for height plyometric — aggressive knee drive and arm action while skipping as high as possible; builds hip extension/flexion and ankle stiffness.
- [Drill skip for distance](drill-skip-for-distance.md) — Skip for distance plyometric — drive knee upward and forward as aggressively as possible to maximize horizontal distance; builds hip power and stride length.
- [Drill split squat jumps](drill-split-squat-jumps.md) — Split-squat jumps plyometric — repeated lunge-position vertical jumps without knee touching the ground; builds hip power and stride length.
- [Drill bounding](drill-bounding.md) — Bounding plyometric — exaggerated running with knee driven to thigh-parallel and a slight jump each stride; builds hip extension/flexion and ankle stiffness.
- [Drill single leg bounds](drill-single-leg-bounds.md) — Single-leg bounds plyometric — continuous single-leg hopping with sprint-mechanics leg recovery; builds hip strength and stride length, measurable by distance per hops.
- [Drill high knees](drill-high-knees.md) — High knees plyometric drill — thigh-to-parallel marching in place with foot dorsiflexion; develops sprint technique's high knee drive. Variation: Backward Knees.
- [Drill 4x4s](drill-4x4s.md) — 4×4s plyometric — alternating high knees and butt-kickers, each performed 4 times over 33 yards; increases hip flexor range of motion and stride length.
- [Drill heel and toe walks](drill-heel-and-toe-walks.md) — Heel and toe walks gait strength drill — heel walks develop anterior tibialis and correct dorsiflexion; toe walks build calf strength; both prevent shin splints.
- [Drill galloping](drill-galloping.md) — Galloping gait strength drill — trailing ankle locked 'spring-loaded' takeoff; promotes hip projection, back leg push-off, and pawing leg-cycle mechanics.
- [Drill pool drills](drill-pool-drills.md) — Pool drills resistance exercise — performing sprint drills in chest-high or shallow water for recovery, injury training, and resistance with reduced impact.
- [Drill pit smashers](drill-pit-smashers.md) — Pit smashers acceleration drill — explosive drive out of blocks into a high-jump pit 4 feet away; develops aggressive low-angle start and full hip/knee/ankle extension.
- [Drill carioca](drill-carioca.md) — Carioca lateral crossover footwork drill — develops hip flexibility, balance, footwork coordination, and lateral speed for basketball.
- [Drill crossover skipping](drill-crossover-skipping.md) — Crossover skipping lateral drill — develops explosive crossover mechanics, contralateral hip flexion/extension, and direction-change power for basketball.
- [Drill 20 yard shuttle](drill-20-yard-shuttle.md) — 20-Yard Shuttle line sprint — improves change-of-direction ability, footwork, and reaction time with 5-yard and 10-yard sprint/touch sequences.
- [Drill 30 yard t drill](drill-30-yard-t-drill.md) — 30-Yard T-Drill — develops agility, conditioning, and hip abductor/adductor flexibility through a sprint-shuffle T-pattern with backpedal finish.
- [Drill squirm](drill-squirm.md) — Squirm line sprint drill — develops footwork and reaction time through sprint segments interrupted by 360-degree rotations, with lateral sprint finish.
- [Drill 40 yard sprint agility](drill-40-yard-sprint-agility.md) — 40-Yard Sprint agility line drill — develops agility and conditioning through repeated 5-yard and 10-yard sprint-touch-return sequences in a multi-line pattern.
- [Drill 60 yard shuttle sprint](drill-60-yard-shuttle-sprint.md) — 60-Yard Shuttle Sprint — improves agility and conditioning through three progressively longer sprint-touch-return legs (5, 10, 15 yards).
- [Drill 40 yard lateral shuffle](drill-40-yard-lateral-shuffle.md) — 40-Yard Lateral Shuffle line drill — improves agility, conditioning, and hip abductor/adductor flexibility through a purely lateral shuffle pattern.
- [Drill 40 yard backpedal forward](drill-40-yard-backpedal-forward.md) — 40-Yard Backpedal-Forward line drill — improves agility, direction-change ability, and conditioning through alternating backpedal-to-sprint transitions.
- [Drill 55 yard sprint backpedal](drill-55-yard-sprint-backpedal.md) — 55-Yard Sprint-Backpedal line drill — develops acceleration and stopping ability through four alternating sprint/backpedal intervals with specific coaching cues for forward lean and braking.
- [Drill 100 yard sprint agility](drill-100-yard-sprint-agility.md) — 100-Yard Sprint agility line drill — improves change-of-direction, footwork, and reaction time through four progressively longer sprint-touch-return intervals (5, 10, 15, 20 yards).
- [Drill 40 yard square carioca](drill-40-yard-square-carioca.md) — 40-Yard Square–Carioca cone drill — combines sprint, carioca, backpedal, and reverse pivots around a 10x10-yard square to improve direction-change ability, hip flexibility, and footwork.
- [Drill 15 yard turn drill](drill-15-yard-turn-drill.md) — 15-Yard Turn Drill — cone drill developing sharp turning ability, hip flexibility, and footwork through a triangular sprint pattern with right and left turns.
- [Drill 20 yard square cone](drill-20-yard-square-cone.md) — 20-Yard Square cone drill — develops direction-change ability, body position transitions, and cutting through a four-cone sprint-shuffle-backpedal-shuffle square pattern.
- [Drill x pattern multiskill](drill-x-pattern-multiskill.md) — X-Pattern Multiskill cone drill — improves transitional movement and cutting ability through diagonal sprints and backpedals in an X-pattern with inside/outside foot plant cues.
- [Drill figure eights](drill-figure-eights.md) — Figure Eights cone drill — improves direction-change ability and reaction time by running a continuous figure-eight pattern around two cones 5-10 yards apart.
- [Drill z pattern run](drill-z-pattern-run.md) — Z-Pattern Run cone drill — improves transitional movement and turning ability through diagonal sprints around alternating cones in a zigzag Z-shaped layout.
- [Drill zigzag cone](drill-zigzag-cone.md) — Zigzag Cone Drill (#68): lateral shuffle through 10 cones 1 yard apart — builds defensive footwork and lateral quickness for basketball.
- [Drill z pattern cuts](drill-z-pattern-cuts.md) — Z-Pattern Cuts Cone Drill (#69): sprint and sharp-angle cuts through a 5×10 yard Z-shaped cone layout — builds cutting ability and change of direction.
- [Drill 40 yard square bear crawl backpedal](drill-40-yard-square-bear-crawl-backpedal.md) — 40-Yard Square Drill — Sprint, Bear Crawl, Backpedal (#70): 10×10 yard square combining sprint, bear crawl, and backpedal to train body-position transitions and direction changes.
- [Drill 40 yard square single leg hop backpedal](drill-40-yard-square-single-leg-hop-backpedal.md) — 40-Yard Square Drill — Sprint, Single-Leg Hop, Backpedal (#71): 10×10 yard square with sprint, single-leg lateral hop, and backpedal — builds unilateral power and direction-change ability.
- [Drill star drill sprint backpedal shuffle](drill-star-drill-sprint-backpedal-shuffle.md) — Star Drill — Sprint, Backpedal, Shuffle (#72): 5-cone star pattern with diagonal sprints, backpedals, and lateral shuffles — comprehensive multi-directional agility drill.
- [Drill star drill sprint carioca backpedal](drill-star-drill-sprint-carioca-backpedal.md) — Star Drill — Sprint, Carioca, Backpedal (#73): 5-cone star pattern replacing shuffles with carioca — builds hip mobility and rotational footwork for defense.
- [Drill star drill sprint bear crawl shuffle](drill-star-drill-sprint-bear-crawl-shuffle.md) — Star Drill — Sprint, Bear Crawl, Shuffle (#74): 5-cone star pattern with diagonal sprints, bear crawls, and lateral shuffles — trains body-position transitions in multiple directions.
- [Drill five cone snake](drill-five-cone-snake.md) — Five-Cone Snake Drill (#75): sprint-only snake pattern through a 10×10 yard 5-cone layout — trains cutting ability and direction change at high speed.
- [Drill s drill cone](drill-s-drill-cone.md) — S-Drill Cone Drill (#76): sprint diagonally around 4 cones in an S-shape (10 yards forward, 5 yards offset) and return — trains cutting, direction change, and curvilinear speed.
- [Drill 10 cone snake](drill-10-cone-snake.md) — 10-Cone Snake Drill (#77): 10-cone layout combining lateral shuffles and diagonal sprints — builds shuffle-to-cut transitions critical for basketball defense.
- [Drill v drill cone](drill-v-drill-cone.md) — V-Drill Cone Drill (#78): sprint diagonally to left cone, backpedal to start, sprint diagonally to right cone, backpedal to start — trains forward-backward direction change off a planted foot.
- [Drill a movement cone](drill-a-movement-cone.md) — A-Movement Cone Drill (#79): 5-cone A-shape drill combining sprint, lateral shuffle, and backpedal — multi-directional agility in a compact 10×5 yard space.
- [Drill e movement cone](drill-e-movement-cone.md) — E-Movement Cone Drill (#80): 6-cone E-shape drill with sprint, shuffle, and backpedal — more complex than A-Movement with two additional shuffle levels.
- [Drill h movement cone](drill-h-movement-cone.md) — H-Movement Cone Drill (#81): 6-cone H-shape drill with sprint, backpedal, and shuffle — trains vertical and lateral multi-directional agility in basketball-specific distances.
- [Drill icky shuffle ladder](drill-icky-shuffle-ladder.md) — Icky Shuffle Agility Ladder Drill (#82): lateral 2-in-1-out footwork pattern through an agility ladder — enhances lower-body coordination and quickness.
- [Drill in out shuffle ladder](drill-in-out-shuffle-ladder.md) — In-Out Shuffle Agility Ladder Drill (#83): standing sideways to ladder, stepping both feet in then both feet out diagonally — improves agility, balance, coordination, and quickness.
- [Drill side right in ladder](drill-side-right-in-ladder.md) — Side Right-In Agility Ladder Drill (#84): lateral stepping pattern with one foot crossing forward over the ladder — improves agility, balance, coordination, and quickness.
- [Drill crossover shuffle ladder](drill-crossover-shuffle-ladder.md) — Crossover Shuffle Agility Ladder Drill (#85): alternating crossover steps through the ladder with only one foot inside at a time — increases hip flexibility and direction-change power.
- [Drill zigzag crossover shuffle ladder](drill-zigzag-crossover-shuffle-ladder.md) — Zigzag Crossover Shuffle Agility Ladder Drill (#86): crossover and behind-the-leg steps weaving through the ladder — develops abductor/adductor flexibility, footwork, and direction-change ability.
- [Drill snake jump ladder](drill-snake-jump-ladder.md) — Snake Jump Agility Ladder Drill (#87): two-feet-together quarter-turn jumps through the ladder — improves agility, balance, coordination, hip flexibility, and quickness via rotational jumps.
- [Drill medicine ball bull in a ring](drill-medicine-ball-bull-in-a-ring.md) — Medicine-Ball Bull in a Ring: two partners face each other and chest-pass a medicine ball while moving in a circle — builds quickness, elastic strength, and reactive passing.
- [Drill medicine ball wall chest pass](drill-medicine-ball-wall-chest-pass.md) — Medicine-ball wall chest pass: rapid two-hand chest passes against a wall improving total-body power transmission. [S8, p.157]
- [Drill medicine ball release pushup partner](drill-medicine-ball-release-pushup-partner.md) — Medicine-ball release push-up with partner: throw med ball from kneeling → fall into push-up → push back up → catch return; upper-body quickness. [S8, p.158]
- [Drill rope skipping plyometric](drill-rope-skipping-plyometric.md) — Rope skipping lower-body plyometric: jump rope to designated spots (bilateral or single-leg) — builds elastic strength and quickness in the lower body. [S8, p.166]
- [Drill vertical jump plyometric](drill-vertical-jump-plyometric.md) — Vertical jump plyometric drill: bilateral counter-movement jump with triple extension and arm reach — foundational lower-body power and quickness drill. [S8, p.171]
- [Drill lunge with power up jump](drill-lunge-with-power-up-jump.md) — Lunge with power-up jump lower-body plyometric — drive off front leg from lunge into a forward two-foot landing, alternating legs for power and quickness.
- [Drill quick feet agility ladder](drill-quick-feet-agility-ladder.md) — Quick Feet (in All Directions) — half agility ladder drill with one foot per rung; emphasizes first-step stride frequency, not linear speed; reaction command variation adds sport-specific stimulus.
- [Drill half ladder sport specific skill](drill-half-ladder-sport-specific-skill.md) — Half ladder skill to sport-specific skill — perform any agility ladder drill while reacting to a coach throwing a ball mid-run; bridges footwork training and sport-specific reaction.
- [Drill reactive push ups with clap](drill-reactive-push-ups-with-clap.md) — Reactive push-ups with clap — two athletes in push-up position 1 yard apart; one performs a clap push-up and the partner reacts to mirror the movement simultaneously; trains upper-body power and reaction.
- [Drill containing opponent drill](drill-containing-opponent-drill.md) — Containing-opponent drill — 3-4 defenders form a wall moving laterally and backpedaling to contain a single athlete sprinting to break through their line over 80 yards.
- [Drill mirroring two box drill](drill-mirroring-two-box-drill.md) — Mirroring two-box drill — two athletes each in a 5-yard cone box; one sprints to random cones and returns to center, the other mirrors; trains reactive change-of-direction speed.
- [Drill triangle drills with commands](drill-triangle-drills-with-commands.md) — Triangle drills with commands — sprint a 3-cone triangle (5-yard sides), changing direction every 2–4 turns on coach's verbal command; complex variation adds a partner chaser.
- [Drill standing stationary arm swings](drill-standing-stationary-arm-swings.md) — Standing stationary arm swings — teaches proper arm mechanics for sprinting in a controlled position; foundational speed technique drill with seated and weighted variations.
- [Drill ankling](drill-ankling.md) — Ankling — short-step jogging drill that builds foot speed and elastic ankle strength through rapid ball-of-foot contacts; foundational speed mechanics drill.
- [Drill straight leg shuffle](drill-straight-leg-shuffle.md) — Straight-leg shuffle — running drill with legs kept straight and foot dorsiflexed to build hip strength and elastic ankle strength for sprinting.
- [Drill butt kickers](drill-butt-kickers.md) — Butt-kickers — jogging drill pulling heel to gluteus to increase foot speed and improve stride cycle recovery mechanics.
- [Drill wall slides](drill-wall-slides.md) — Wall slides — butt-kicker variation keeping recovery heel forward to improve knee lift and increase stride turnover frequency.
- [Drill a march walk](drill-a-march-walk.md) — A-March Walk — supplemental speed drill building foot speed and high knee mechanics through slow marching with perfect posture and plantar flexion emphasis.
- [Drill a skips](drill-a-skips.md) — A-Skips — skipping version of A-March Walk that builds hip extension/flexion strength and ankle stiffness; key drill in the sprint mechanics progression.
- [Drill b march walk](drill-b-march-walk.md) — B-March Walk — supplemental speed drill improving hip-extension mechanics and hamstring firing through high-knee march with forward leg extension and hip drive.
- [Drill b skips](drill-b-skips.md) — B-Skips — skipping version of B-March Walk increasing stride length/frequency and ankle stiffness through B-form leg mechanics with explosive hip drive.
- [Drill ladder speed run](drill-ladder-speed-run.md) — Ladder speed run — two-feet-per-rung agility ladder drill building stride frequency and foot quickness through rapid high-knee contacts.
- [Drill ladder stride run](drill-ladder-stride-run.md) — Ladder stride run — one-foot-per-every-other-rung agility ladder drill building stride frequency and timing at near-sprint speed with upright posture.
- [Drill 180 degree turn ladder](drill-180-degree-turn-ladder.md) — 180-Degree Turn agility ladder drill — bilateral jump and rotate 180° straddling each rung, building agility, balance, and hip flexibility.
- [Drill bag weave](drill-bag-weave.md) — Bag Weave agility drill — sprint, shuffle, and backpedal pattern through 4 bags in a continuous sequence to build flexibility, high-knee action, and foot quickness.
- [Drill combo sidestep forward back](drill-combo-sidestep-forward-back.md) — Combo Sidestep/Forward-Back bag drill — changes direction through 7 bags combining lateral steps, 5-yard sprints, and backpedals to build multi-directional agility.
- [Drill lateral weave bags](drill-lateral-weave-bags.md) — Lateral Weave bag drill — rapid lateral sidestep through 3-4 bags with immediate direction reversal, then sprint 5 yards; builds foot quickness and reaction time.
- [Drill bag hops 180 turn](drill-bag-hops-180-turn.md) — Bag Hops With 180-Degree Turn — bilateral lateral hops over 4-6 bags with 180° mid-air rotation on each hop, combining plyometric training with hip flexibility and foot quickness.
- [Drill wheel bag](drill-wheel-bag.md) — Wheel bag drill — 4 bags in X formation, player sidestepping around all 4 bags clockwise then counterclockwise while keeping hands in the center, then sprint 5 yards; builds balance and foot quickness.
- [Drill side to side skiers angle board](drill-side-to-side-skiers-angle-board.md) — Side-to-Side Skiers angle-board drill — bilateral mid-air rotation landing on alternating angle boards to develop agility and rotational change of direction.
- [Drill side to side skiers slide board](drill-side-to-side-skiers-slide-board.md) — Side-to-Side Skiers With Front/Back Rotation slide-board drill — lateral glide with mid-air counterclockwise or clockwise rotation to build lateral agility and rotational balance.
- [Drill forward roll over shoulder](drill-forward-roll-over-shoulder.md) — Forward Roll Over Shoulder tumbling drill — fall forward and roll over one shoulder back to feet; develops total-body agility and kinesthetic awareness.
- [Drill backward roll over shoulder](drill-backward-roll-over-shoulder.md) — Backward Roll Over Shoulder tumbling drill — sit back, roll over shoulder, return to feet; develops total-body agility and kinesthetic awareness.
- [Drill backward roll hand push off](drill-backward-roll-hand-push-off.md) — Backward Roll to Hand Push-Off tumbling drill — roll back and use hands overhead to push off the ground and return to feet; develops agility and kinesthetic awareness.
- [Drill forward backward roll combo](drill-forward-backward-roll-combo.md) — Forward Roll–Backward Roll Combination tumbling drill — seamlessly chain a forward roll into an immediate backward hand push-off roll; develops agility and kinesthetic awareness.
- [Drill cartwheel tumbling](drill-cartwheel-tumbling.md) — Cartwheel tumbling drill — lateral hand-to-ground rotational movement through 360° returning to feet; develops total-body agility and kinesthetic awareness.
- [Drill round off tumbling](drill-round-off-tumbling.md) — Round-Off tumbling drill — cartwheel variation where both feet land simultaneously facing the starting direction; develops total-body agility and kinesthetic awareness.
- [Drill tumbling variations](drill-tumbling-variations.md) — Tumbling Drill Variations — running start over barrier and tumbling sequencing progressions that increase amplitude, difficulty, and kinesthetic demands of all tumbling drills.
- [Drill drop and get up](drill-drop-and-get-up.md) — Drop and Get Up crazy Z-ball drill — throw a Z-ball in the air, drop to the floor for a push-up, then scramble up to catch the ball before it bounces twice; builds reaction time and change-of-direction ability.
- [Drill hexagon drill](drill-hexagon-drill.md) — Hexagon Drill — timed bilateral jumps outside each of 6 sides of a taped hexagon (clockwise and counterclockwise) to improve overall agility.
- [Drill toss get up catch](drill-toss-get-up-catch.md) — Toss, Get Up, and Catch medicine-ball drill — lie on back, chest-pass medicine ball overhead, scramble to feet, and catch before it hits the ground; improves level-change capability and power-to-agility transition.
- [Drill single leg balance opposite leg reach](drill-single-leg-balance-opposite-leg-reach.md) — Single-Leg Balance With Opposite-Leg Reach — unilateral stance drill with anterior, posterior, and medial leg reaches to build single-leg balance for basketball cutting and landing.
- [Drill single leg balance opposite arm reach](drill-single-leg-balance-opposite-arm-reach.md) — Single-Leg Balance With Opposite-Arm Reach — unilateral stance drill using arms as drivers through multiple reach vectors (waist, foot, overhead) to build advanced single-leg balance.
- [Drill single leg balance dumbbell press](drill-single-leg-balance-dumbbell-press.md) — Single-Leg Balance Dumbbell Presses — overhead dumbbell presses in multiple tri-plane patterns while balancing on one leg, combining upper-body strength with single-leg balance challenge.
- [Drill hop and stick balance](drill-hop-and-stick-balance.md) — Hop-and-stick balance drills — dynamic single-leg landing holds in four directions over 10 yards; variable stick count and head-turning progressions.
- [Drill lunge patterns](drill-lunge-patterns.md) — Multi-plane lunge patterns — anterior, lateral, and transverse lunges for lower-extremity strength, hip range of motion, and dynamic balance.
- [Drill backpedal quickness](drill-backpedal-quickness.md) — Backpedal drill — athletic-stance backward running to improve hip flexor quickness and flexibility; open-step sprint-to-cone variation for reaction training.
- [Drill multidirectional skipping](drill-multidirectional-skipping.md) — Multidirectional skipping drill — skip forward, backward, and laterally on command while facing a target; trains quickness and locomotive coordination.
- [Drill medicine ball bull in ring](drill-medicine-ball-bull-in-ring.md) — Medicine-Ball Bull in a Ring — partners face each other chest-passing a medicine ball while moving in a circle; builds quickness and elastic strength.
- [Drill medicine ball lateral shuffle pass](drill-medicine-ball-lateral-shuffle-pass.md) — Medicine-Ball Lateral Shuffle/Pass — partners shuffle laterally while chest-passing a medicine ball; builds quickness and elastic strength for defensive slides.
- [Drill medicine ball squat push toss](drill-medicine-ball-squat-push-toss.md) — Medicine-Ball Squat, Push Toss, Bounce, and Catch — squat with medicine ball, throw for height and distance, sprint to catch before second bounce; builds reactive total-body power.
- [Drill medicine ball forward scoop toss](drill-medicine-ball-forward-scoop-toss.md) — Medicine-Ball Forward Scoop Toss, Bounce, and Catch — between-legs squat swing and forward toss followed by sprint to catch before second bounce; total-body power and reactive strength.
- [Drill ball drops with partner](drill-ball-drops-with-partner.md) — Ball Drops With a Partner — partner drops a ball from shoulder height 5–10 yards away; reactor must sprint and catch after first bounce; trains visual stimulus response and first-step quickness.
- [Drill goalie reaction](drill-goalie-reaction.md) — Goalie Drill — defender in wide athletic stance stops a rolling ball from crossing a goal line using hands, feet, or any combination; trains upper-body quickness and reactive lateral movement.
- [Drill partner blind tosses](drill-partner-blind-tosses.md) — Partner Blind Tosses — partner tosses a ball from behind over one shoulder; reactor sprints to catch before second bounce; builds upper and lower-body quickness and pure visual reaction speed.
- [Drill stability ball cyclic impact lockouts](drill-stability-ball-cyclic-impact-lockouts.md) — Stability-Ball Cyclic Impact Lockouts — plank on stability ball, release and fall onto abdominals, bounce off ball and lockout arms; strengthens core and trains the body to absorb and redirect impact forces.
- [Drill stability ball hops](drill-stability-ball-hops.md) — Stability-ball hops — upper-body quickness drill in push-up position with feet on a stability ball, hopping backward/forward and side to side.
- [Drill wheelbarrow drill](drill-wheelbarrow-drill.md) — Wheelbarrow Drill — partner-assisted upper-body plyometric where one athlete walks/runs/jumps on hands while partner holds feet; builds upper-body power and core.
- [Drill plyo push ups](drill-plyo-push-ups.md) — Plyo Push-Ups — explosive push-up where hands leave the ground; builds upper-body quickness and reactive pushing power for basketball actions.
- [Drill medicine ball wall chest passes](drill-medicine-ball-wall-chest-passes.md) — Medicine-Ball Wall Chest Passes — upper-body plyometric passing drill against a wall to improve total-body power transmission and passing explosiveness.
- [Drill medicine ball release push ups partner](drill-medicine-ball-release-push-ups-partner.md) — Medicine-Ball Release Push-Ups With Partner — kneeling throw to a partner followed immediately by a push-up; builds upper-body pushing quickness and power.
- [Drill medicine ball wall side toss](drill-medicine-ball-wall-side-toss.md) — Medicine-Ball Wall Side Toss — rotational medicine ball throw against a wall to develop explosive rotational mechanics and direction-change power.
- [Drill medicine ball overhead throw](drill-medicine-ball-overhead-throw.md) — Medicine-Ball Overhead Throw — bilateral overhead wall throw to improve explosive power in throwing and overhead basketball actions (rebounding, shot-blocking, passing).
- [Drill medicine ball wall scoop toss](drill-medicine-ball-wall-scoop-toss.md) — Medicine-Ball Wall Scoop Toss — squat-and-extend medicine ball toss against wall to enhance total-body extension, quickness, and power.
- [Drill upper body shuffles](drill-upper-body-shuffles.md) — Upper-Body Shuffles — push-up plyometric where hands shuffle positions during the airborne phase; develops upper-body quickness and lateral reaction speed.
- [Drill medicine ball one arm push off](drill-medicine-ball-one-arm-push-off.md) — Medicine-Ball One-Arm Push-Off — unilateral plyometric push-up with one hand on a medicine ball; builds single-arm explosive power and reactive quickness.
- [Drill medicine ball upper body shuffles](drill-medicine-ball-upper-body-shuffles.md) — Medicine-Ball Upper-Body Shuffles — lateral push-up plyometric where the athlete's body traverses over a medicine ball, building lateral upper-body power and quickness.
- [Drill upper body box shuffles](drill-upper-body-box-shuffles.md) — Upper-Body Box Shuffles — push-up plyometric on a box; hands start on box, drop to straddle the box, then explosively return; builds upper-body reactive quickness.
- [Drill explosive reclined pulls](drill-explosive-reclined-pulls.md) — Explosive Reclined Pulls — upper-body plyometric pulling drill using a thick rope at 45° body recline; builds explosive pulling power for rebounding and defense.
- [Drill rope skipping](drill-rope-skipping.md) — Rope-Skipping — lower-body plyometric drill building elastic strength and quickness via continuous jump rope with bilateral or unilateral, stationary or directional patterns.
- [Drill in place ankle jumps](drill-in-place-ankle-jumps.md) — In-Place Ankle Jumps — stationary lower-body plyometric using only ankle plantar flexion to build elastic strength and quickness for rapid court movement.
- [Drill scissor jumps](drill-scissor-jumps.md) — Scissor Jumps — alternating single-leg forward kick jumps to improve hip quickness, balance, and the explosive leg-drive pattern used in layups and fast-break strides.
- [Drill lateral skaters](drill-lateral-skaters.md) — Lateral Skaters — single-leg lateral bound plyometric building cutting ability and first-step lateral quickness directly applicable to defensive slides and offensive drives.
- [Drill in place tuck jumps](drill-in-place-tuck-jumps.md) — In-Place Tuck Jumps — bilateral lower-body plyometric with knee tuck at peak height; builds vertical power, reactive strength, and second-jump ability for rebounding.
- [Drill vertical jump s8](drill-vertical-jump-s8.md) — Vertical Jump plyometric drill — bilateral explosive jump from pre-stretch position with triple extension and arm reach; includes reactive variation for second-jump training.
- [Drill standing long jump](drill-standing-long-jump.md) — Standing Long Jump — bilateral lower-body plyometric projecting horizontally for distance; builds explosive lower-body power for acceleration and fast-break first steps.
