- [Drill barrier jumps](drill-barrier-jumps.md) — Barrier Jumps — bilateral plyometric jumps over hurdles/cones/boxes building lower-body power and quickness; includes lateral and single-leg variations.
- [Drill power skips](drill-power-skips.md) — Power skips lower-body plyometric — aggressive hip extension skips maximizing distance and height with minimal ground contact time.
- [Drill lunge power up jump](drill-lunge-power-up-jump.md) — Lunge with power-up jump plyometric — forward lunge into a two-foot explosive jump, alternating legs, building lower-body power and quickness.
- [Drill barrier jump cut sprint](drill-barrier-jump-cut-sprint.md) — Barrier jump with cut and sprint — jump a hurdle then react to a coach signal to sprint left or right; builds reactive lower-body power and first-step quickness.
- [Drill push off box shuffle](drill-push-off-box-shuffle.md) — Push-off box shuffle plyometric — alternate feet on/off a low box with stiff ankle landing to build elastic ankle strength and lower-body quickness.
- [Drill jump rope multidirectional](drill-jump-rope-multidirectional.md) — Jump rope with multidirectional jumps — alternating straddle and split-foot positions while jumping rope to improve lower-body power and quickness.
- [Drill sequence jumping jacks](drill-sequence-jumping-jacks.md) — Sequence jumping jacks lower-body plyometric — alternating wide and split-foot jumping jack patterns with optional crossover variation to build lower-body quickness.
- [Drill quick feet all directions](drill-quick-feet-all-directions.md) — Quick feet in all directions — half agility ladder drill with one-foot-per-rung pattern and reaction command sprint to enhance first-step stride frequency.
- [Drill bunny jumps ladder](drill-bunny-jumps-ladder.md) — Bunny jumps half agility ladder drill — fast double-foot jumps into every ladder square with minimal ground contact to build ankle complex elastic strength.
- [Drill hop scotch ladder](drill-hop-scotch-ladder.md) — Hop-scotch half agility ladder drill — alternating feet-together and feet-apart jumps through the ladder, with single-leg variation, to build ankle elastic strength.
- [Drill one leg hop ladder](drill-one-leg-hop-ladder.md) — One-leg hop half agility ladder drill — single-leg hops through every ladder square minimizing ground contact to improve unilateral lower-body quickness.
- [Drill half ladder skill to sport skill](drill-half-ladder-skill-to-sport-skill.md) — Half ladder skill to sport-specific skill — athlete runs any ladder drill while reacting mid-run to a ball thrown by coach; bridges footwork training and sport skill.
- [Drill ruler drop test](drill-ruler-drop-test.md) — Ruler drop test — partner drops a ruler from shoulder height for the athlete to catch, measuring upper-body quickness and reaction time to a stimulus.
- [Drill reactive push ups clap](drill-reactive-push-ups-clap.md) — Reactive push-ups with clap — two athletes in push-up position react to each other's movement to perform synchronized clap push-ups, building upper-body power and reaction.
- [Drill partner resisted lateral shuffle chase](drill-partner-resisted-lateral-shuffle-chase.md) — Partner-resisted lateral shuffle and chase — partner resists a side-shuffle then releases and sprints; athlete chases and tags; builds directional quickness and reaction.
- [Drill mirroring partner sprints](drill-mirroring-partner-sprints.md) — Mirroring partner sprints — athlete sprints 10 yards while partner backpedals the same distance, then reverses, maintaining gap; builds reactive direction change.
- [Drill containing opponent](drill-containing-opponent.md) — Containing-opponent drill — athlete tries to break through a 3-4 person defensive wall over 80 yards; defenders backpedal and shuffle laterally to contain; builds reactive direction change.
- [Drill mirroring two box](drill-mirroring-two-box.md) — Mirroring two-box drill — two athletes in separate cone boxes sprint to any cone and return to center; partner must mirror every movement; builds reactive direction change.
- [Drill mirror drills box square shuffle](drill-mirror-drills-box-square-shuffle.md) — Mirror drills in box with square shuffle — two athletes shuffle on the perimeter lines of adjacent boxes; commander leads, reactor mirrors; builds lateral quickness and reactive ability.
- [Drill triangle drills commands](drill-triangle-drills-commands.md) — Triangle drills with commands — sprint around three cones (5 yards apart) changing direction on coach's verbal command every 2–4 turns; builds foot plant quickness and COD.
- [Drill three step foot tap sprint](drill-three-step-foot-tap-sprint.md) — Three-step foot-tap drill with sprint — foot-tap pattern in a hoop then react to coach's signal to sprint to a cone 5 yards away; builds first-step quickness and reaction.
- [Drill dodge ball reaction](drill-dodge-ball-reaction.md) — Dodge Ball whole-body reaction drill — 2-4 players vs wall or 5+ in a circle; evade soft-ball throws to improve mental processing speed and total-body reaction time.
- [Drill rapid fire reaction](drill-rapid-fire-reaction.md) — Rapid Fire whole-body reaction drill — fast foot taps in ready position, then react to coach commands (shuffle, sprint, jump, sprawl) as quickly as possible.
- [Drill barrel roll to reaction](drill-barrel-roll-to-reaction.md) — Barrel Roll to Reaction — forward shoulder roll from a two-point stance, return to ready position, then react to coach's visual/audible cue; builds agility and reaction time.
- [Drill backward roll to reaction](drill-backward-roll-to-reaction.md) — Backward Roll to Reaction — squat into a backward shoulder roll, return to ready position, react to coach's cue; develops whole-body agility and reaction time.
- [Drill skiers with reaction](drill-skiers-with-reaction.md) — Skiers With Reaction agility ladder drill — diagonal jump pattern through the ladder while reacting to coach's visual commands; builds court sense, agility, and peripheral vision.
- [Drill hop scotch with reaction](drill-hop-scotch-with-reaction.md) — Hop-Scotch With Reaction agility ladder drill — bilateral jump pattern (inside-outside-inside) through ladder while reacting to coach's visual commands; builds ankle strength and reaction time.
- [Drill icky shuffle with reaction](drill-icky-shuffle-with-reaction.md) — Icky Shuffle With Reaction agility ladder drill — lateral step pattern through the ladder while reacting to coach's visual commands; builds court sense, quick feet, and mental processing speed.
- [Drill backward icky shuffle with reaction](drill-backward-icky-shuffle-with-reaction.md) — Backward Icky Shuffle With Reaction — reverse icky shuffle pattern (facing backward) through agility ladder while reacting to coach's visual commands; builds backpedal quickness and reaction time.
- [Drill in and out shuffle with reaction](drill-in-and-out-shuffle-with-reaction.md) — In-and-Out Shuffle With Reaction — forward-diagonal step into ladder then diagonal step in front of next square, while reacting to coach's visual commands; builds agility and mental processing speed.
- [Drill snake with reaction](drill-snake-with-reaction.md) — Snake With Reaction agility ladder drill — two-foot quarter-turn jumps straddling the ladder while reacting to coach's commands; builds ankle elasticity, hip rotation, and reaction time.
- [Drill chubby checkers with reaction](drill-chubby-checkers-with-reaction.md) — Chubby Checkers With Reaction agility ladder drill — lateral two-foot jumps in-out-in pattern advancing along ladder while reacting to coach commands; builds first-step quickness and reaction time.
- [Drill defensive slide change direction](drill-defensive-slide-change-direction.md) — Full-court defensive slide and change-of-direction cone drill: players slide, pivot, sprint, and re-slide through 7 cones to build defensive footwork and lateral quickness.
- [Drill 1v1 zigzag defense](drill-1v1-zigzag-defense.md) — 1-on-1 zigzag full-court defensive drill: defender forces the dribbler to change direction repeatedly across the full court by getting a spot in front of the outside hand.
- [Drill 2v2 full court defense](drill-2v2-full-court-defense.md) — 2-on-2 full-court defensive drill: defenders slide through on DHOs and run-and-jump the dribbler, teaching help-and-recover, V-positioning, and ball pressure on exchanges.
- [Drill 3v2 full court fast break defense](drill-3v2-full-court-fast-break-defense.md) — 3-on-2 continuous full-court fast-break defensive drill: two defenders contain three offensive players in tandem until a third defender arrives from mid-court, then play 3v3.
- [Drill 3v3 full court defense](drill-3v3-full-court-defense.md) — 3-on-3 continuous full-court defensive drill (player or coach inbounds): defenders contain offense through DHOs, screens, and weak-side exchanges while communicating on every possession.
- [Drill post defense three quarter fronting](drill-post-defense-three-quarter-fronting.md) — One-on-one post defense drill: three passers move the ball while the post defender practices three-quartering and fronting the low post based on ball position, sitting on the post's legs.
- [Defensive shell drill](defensive-shell-drill.md) — Herb Brown's 4-on-4 half-court shell drill: the cornerstone defensive team drill teaching help positioning, ball movement reaction, screen defense, post defense, and competitive stops — run almost daily throughout the season.
- [Drill defensive slide backpedal pivot run](drill-defensive-slide-backpedal-pivot-run.md) — Defensive footwork pattern drill: slide across the baseline, slide back to the low block, backpedal to the foul line, pivot, and run to the foul line extended — both solo and with a mirror partner.
- [Drill 2 on 1 trapping](drill-2-on-1-trapping.md) — Two-defenders-versus-one-ball-handler trapping drill: contain and trap the dribbler for 8-10 seconds in backcourt or front court corner without fouling.
- [Drill defensive fast break progressions](drill-defensive-fast-break-progressions.md) — Continuous transition defense drill progressing 2v1 → 3v2 → 4v3 → 5v4 → 5v5 on a full court — builds communication, recognition, and ball-stopping habits in all transition scenarios.
- [Drill 4v4 transition defense](drill-4v4-transition-defense.md) — 4-on-4 full-court transition drill: one defender touches the foul line before chasing a 4v3 fast break, training ball-stopping, goal protection, and trailer recovery.
- [Drill fast break off free throw](drill-fast-break-off-free-throw.md) — Full-team drill defending the opponent's fast break immediately after a made or missed free throw — simulates the most common transition trigger in late-game situations.
- [Drill cone shuffle warmup](drill-cone-shuffle-warmup.md) — Cone shuffle warm-up drill series (1–4 cone variations, partner option) building basketball-specific footwork, change of direction, and transition to attack.
- [Drill trapping 2v1](drill-trapping-2v1.md) — 2-on-1 trapping drill: two defenders trap and contain one ball handler for 8-10 seconds in backcourt or near a corner without fouling or being split.
- [Defensive transition drills](defensive-transition-drills.md) — Herb Brown's progressive transition defense drill series: 2v1 through 5v5 continuous, 4v4 full-court, 5v5 live, and fast-break-off-free-throw drills.
- [Drill holton closeout](drill-holton-closeout.md) — Michael Holton's Close-Out Drill: defenders close out on ball, pivot, trace/pressure the ball, then sprint-close-out to the opposite side on a skip pass — 30-second rotations.
- [Drill 3v2 fast break with trailer](drill-3v2-fast-break-with-trailer.md) — Continuous 3-on-2 fast-break drill with a trailer: tandem defense, mid-court touch-and-sprint trailer, competitive to 11 baskets — teaches fast-break defense, rebounding, and conditioning.
- [Drill continuous fast break progression](drill-continuous-fast-break-progression.md) — Continuous full-court fast-break progression drill: 2v1 → 3v2 → 4v3 → 5v4 → 5v5, with players rotating in from hash marks to simulate all transition scenarios.
- [Drill 3v3 4v4 continuous full court](drill-3v3-4v4-continuous-full-court.md) — Three-team or four-team continuous full-court 3v3/4v4 drill: winner stays on defense, loser cycles to end of line — played to a preset number of defensive stops.
- [Drill 3v2 2v1 1v1 continuous](drill-3v2-2v1-1v1-continuous.md) — Continuous fast-break drill cycling 3v2 → 2v1 → 1v1 full-court: each defensive pair/player immediately becomes an offensive unit after the break ends — non-stop transition training.
- [Drill 4v4 half court game of stops](drill-4v4-half-court-game-of-stops.md) — 4-on-4 half-court Game of Stops: defense earns points for stops and stays on — first team to 7 stops wins; coach acts as inbound passer to keep pace high.
- [Basketball warmup drills](basketball-warmup-drills.md) — Advanced basketball warm-up cone drills and supplemental exercises for flexibility, balance, strength, and injury prevention before practice.
- [Drill rip step workout series](drill-rip-step-workout-series.md) — Rip step workout series (#2-1 through #2-5) — progressive individual workouts building all rip step scoring opportunities at game speed from 55 to 260+ shots.
- [Drill rip step stride stop shots](drill-rip-step-stride-stop-shots.md) — Rip step to stride stop pull-up jump shot workout series — 1 and 2 dribble versions, both directions, with free throws interspersed. Three volume levels: 80/120/240 shots.
- [Drill rip step stride stop step through](drill-rip-step-stride-stop-step-through.md) — Rip step to stride stop with a counter step-through layup/floater workout — 1 and 2 dribbles, both directions, with free throws. Three volume levels: 80/120/240 shots.
- [Drill sf stride stop workout](drill-sf-stride-stop-workout.md) — Progressive shot fake (SF) stride stop shooting workouts (Workouts #3-6 through the stride-stop series): 80–240 reps in left/right × 1/2-dribble combinations with FT intervals.
- [Drill sf stride stop step through workout](drill-sf-stride-stop-step-through-workout.md) — Progressive shot fake stride stop/step-through combo workouts (#3-7, #3-8, #3-9): 80–240 reps training the pull-up AND step-through reads off the same fake action.
- [Drill sf big hop workout](drill-sf-big-hop-workout.md) — Progressive shot fake big hop workouts (#3-10, #3-11, #3-12): 80–240 reps training the explosive two-foot gather pull-up off a shot fake in all four L/R × 1/2-dribble combinations.
- [Drill sf hop back workout](drill-sf-hop-back-workout.md) — Progressive shot fake hop back workouts (#3-13, #3-14, #3-15): 40–120 reps training the hop-back three-pointer and hop-back midrange off a shot fake in left/right × 1/2-dribble combinations.
- [Drill sf hop back roll out workout](drill-sf-hop-back-roll-out-workout.md) — Progressive shot fake hop back to roll-out dribble workouts (#3-16, #3-17, #3-18): 40–120 reps training the 3-part fake → hop-back → roll-out counter in all four combinations.
- [Drill sf hop back crossover workout](drill-sf-hop-back-crossover-workout.md) — Shot fake hop back to crossover dribble workout (#3-19): introductory 40-rep workout training the most advanced hop-back counter — hop back then crossover to attack the opposite direction.
- [Drill sf pull up threes workout](drill-sf-pull-up-threes-workout.md) — Progressive shot-fake pull-up three-pointer workout series (Workouts #3-22 to #3-24): 25, 50, and 100 SF pull-up 3PT shots with free throws between every set.
- [Drill combination live ball workouts](drill-combination-live-ball-workouts.md) — Combination live-ball shooting workouts (Workouts #4-1 to #4-5): progressive full-series drills chaining stride stops, step-throughs, big hops, hop-backs, roll-outs, crossovers, and attack layups — both directions.
- [Drill combination hop back crossover workout](drill-combination-hop-back-crossover-workout.md) — Progressive combination live-ball drill series: hop-back to crossover dribble (L and R) in 40/80/120-rep workouts with free throws between sets.
- [Drill fade shot workout](drill-fade-shot-workout.md) — Progressive fade shot drill series off a stationary screen (25/50/100 reps from both sides) — catch on the wing, fade away for a 15-20 ft jump shot.
- [Drill dribble fade workout](drill-dribble-fade-workout.md) — Dribble fade drill: catch on the wing off a screen, read the defender slipping the screen, establish pivot foot, attack baseline with a dribble fade and score.
- [Drill dribble fade shooting](drill-dribble-fade-shooting.md) — Dribble fade drill off a stationary screen: defender closes out high, cutter attacks the baseline with a dribble fade; progressions from 25 to 100+ reps with FT intervals.
- [Drill fill shot off screen](drill-fill-shot-off-screen.md) — Fill shot drill off a stationary screen: catch-and-shoot at 15–20 ft on the wing; progressions from 25 to 100 reps with FT intervals.
- [Drill dribble fill off screen](drill-dribble-fill-off-screen.md) — Dribble fill drill off a screen: defender trails low, cutter attacks the middle of the paint with a dribble fill; 25–100 rep progressions with FT intervals.
- [Drill curl shot off screen](drill-curl-shot-off-screen.md) — Curl shot drill off a stationary screen: shooter curls to the elbow (10–15 ft) for a catch-and-shoot; 25–100 rep progressions with FT intervals.
- [Drill dribble curl off screen](drill-dribble-curl-off-screen.md) — Dribble curl drill: defender trails directly behind cutter, who curls to the elbow and continues dribbling to the middle for any scoring play; 25–100 rep progressions.
- [Drill transition shooting series 10](drill-transition-shooting-series-10.md) — Transition shooting series: 10 consecutive full-court shots (3PT, shot fake, rip step, combination) without stopping — elite conditioning + shooting drill.
- [Drill full court transition 3s](drill-full-court-transition-3s.md) — Full-court transition three-point shooting drill (25 or 50 shots): sprint from half court to 3PT line, shoot, touch baseline, sprint back — elite conditioning + shooting.
- [Drill 1 on 0 box dribbling](drill-1-on-0-box-dribbling.md) — 1-on-0 box dribble drill: player works strong dribble, rocker, rocker-to-crossover, and switch dribble in an imaginary box at top of key for 15–60 seconds.
- [Drill 1 on 1 box dribbling](drill-1-on-1-box-dribbling.md) — 1-on-1 box dribble drill: offensive player works four dribble moves against a live defender in an imaginary box at top of key for 15–60 seconds under maximum pressure.
- [Drill open court dribble moves](drill-open-court-dribble-moves.md) — Full-court open-court dribble moves drill: sprint at a cone near the 3PT line, execute a specific dribble move (roll out, crossover, between legs, behind back), then score.
- [Drill racetrack dribble](drill-racetrack-dribble.md) — The Racetrack: full-court integration drill combining 1-on-1 box dribbling, open-court dribble moves, and a variety of scoring finishes in one continuous sequence.
- [Drill shots a day 300](drill-shots-a-day-300.md) — 300+ Shots-a-Day Club daily workout: 308 total shots mixing spot shots, SF/Rip Step series, game-speed 3s, and 60 free throws with documented make targets.
- [Drill shots a day 500](drill-shots-a-day-500.md) — 500+ Shots-a-Day Club daily workout: 520 total shots (doubled reps from 300+ Club) with 120 free throws and 120 game-speed 3PTs; elite-level daily volume benchmark.
- [Drill spot shot workout series](drill-spot-shot-workout-series.md) — Progressive solo spot-shot workout series (50–125 shots) alternating outside shooting with free throws — full-speed, self-rebounding, no shots inside 5 feet.
- [Drill follow leader shooting](drill-follow-leader-shooting.md) — Follow-the-leader partner shooting framework: one player leads a shot, the next player copies the exact same shot — scalable from 2 to 20 players for spot shots, 3PT, or live-ball moves.
- [Drill favorite spot make goals](drill-favorite-spot-make-goals.md) — Make-goal solo shooting workouts at a player's 3 strongest spots: make 10, 20, or 30 shots per spot regardless of attempts — builds confidence and spot mastery through accountability.
- [Drill weakest spot make goals](drill-weakest-spot-make-goals.md) — Make-goal solo shooting workouts at a player's 3 weakest spots: make 10, 20, or 30 shots per spot regardless of attempts — deliberately attacks shooting deficiencies to eliminate cold zones.
- [Drill wing to top combo live ball](drill-wing-to-top-combo-live-ball.md) — Wing-to-Top Combo Live-Ball Move drill: two-foot stop catch past the arc, execute a combination live-ball move, then shoot — both sides at game speed.
- [Drill wing to top rip step live ball](drill-wing-to-top-rip-step-live-ball.md) — Wing-to-Top Rip Step Live-Ball Move drill: two-foot stop catch at the arc, rip step through defender, shoot — both sides at game speed with charting.
- [Drill wing to top shot fake live ball](drill-wing-to-top-shot-fake-live-ball.md) — Wing-to-Top Shot Fake Live-Ball Move drill: two-foot stop catch at the arc, use a shot fake to freeze defender, attack off the live dribble — both sides, game speed.
- [Drill rip step workouts](drill-rip-step-workouts.md) — Progressive rip step individual workout series (Workouts #2-1 through #2-5): 55–260+ shot structured sessions covering all rip step scoring variations with built-in free throws and progress charts.
- [Drill rip step stride stop](drill-rip-step-stride-stop.md) — Rip step into a stride-stop pull-up jump shot — 1 or 2 dribble version, both directions, with free throw breaks between sets.
- [Drill rip step step through](drill-rip-step-step-through.md) — Rip step into stride stop with a step-through layup read — player reads defender recovery and chooses pull-up or continues through for a layup.
- [Drill rip step big hop](drill-rip-step-big-hop.md) — Rip step into a two-foot big hop gather for contact finishing near the rim — 1 and 2 dribble versions, both directions, with FT breaks.
- [Drill rip step hop back](drill-rip-step-hop-back.md) — Rip step into a hop-back retreat three-pointer — 1 and 2 dribble versions creating space from a collapsing defender for an open 3-point shot.
- [Drill rip step hop back roll out](drill-rip-step-hop-back-roll-out.md) — Rip step hop back followed immediately by a roll-out dribble — the counter when the defender lunges at the hop-back shot to attack a new angle.
- [Drill rip step hop back crossover](drill-rip-step-hop-back-crossover.md) — Rip step hop-back to crossover dribble shooting drill series — builds pull-up, hop-back 3, and crossover combo off live-ball rip moves (workouts 2-19 to 2-21).
- [Drill rip step pull up 3s](drill-rip-step-pull-up-3s.md) — Rip step pull-up three-point shooting drill series (25, 50, 100 shots) — trains the off-dribble three-point shot created by a rip-step live-ball move.
- [Drill shot fake full workout series](drill-shot-fake-full-workout-series.md) — Comprehensive shot fake/step fake workout series (Workouts 3-1 to 3-5) covering all scoring moves: stride stop, step-through, big hop, hop back, roll out, crossover, attack lay-ups, and game-speed 3s.
- [Drill combo stride stop shot](drill-combo-stride-stop-shot.md) — Live-ball stride stop combination shooting drill — 1 or 2 dribbles into a two-foot stride stop jump shot, both directions, with FT clusters; 80/120/240 shot progressions.
- [Drill combo stride stop step through](drill-combo-stride-stop-step-through.md) — Live-ball stride stop / step-through combination drill — reads the shot fake into a step-through layup off 1–2 dribbles, both directions, with FT clusters; 80/120/240 progressions.
- [Drill combo big hop](drill-combo-big-hop.md) — Live-ball big hop combination shooting drill — wide two-foot hop gather into a jump shot off 1–2 dribbles, both directions, with FT clusters; 80/120/240 shot progressions.
- [Drill combo hop back](drill-combo-hop-back.md) — Live-ball hop back combination drill — backward hop to create space for a three-pointer or midrange pull-up off 1–2 dribbles, both directions; 40/80/120 shot progressions.
- [Drill combo hop back roll out](drill-combo-hop-back-roll-out.md) — Live-ball hop-back / roll-out combination drill — hop back to create space, then roll the ball forward to re-attack off the live dribble when the defender follows; 40/80/120 progressions.
- [Drill combo hop back crossover](drill-combo-hop-back-crossover.md) — Live-ball hop-back / crossover combination drill — hop back to create space, then crossover dribble to attack the opposite direction when defender follows; 40-shot beginner version.
- [Drill hop back crossover combo workout](drill-hop-back-crossover-combo-workout.md) — Progressive live-ball combination workouts (40–120 reps) cycling through hop-back and crossover dribble pull-up shots with free throws between sets.
- [Drill combo pull up 3pt workout](drill-combo-pull-up-3pt-workout.md) — Progressive live-ball combination pull-up three-point shot workouts (25, 50, 100 reps) with free throws between sets — targets 60% 3PT and 85% FT.
- [Drill combinations in the clutch](drill-combinations-in-the-clutch.md) — Competitive 130-shot clutch workout cycling all combination live-ball moves with a 97/148-point threshold to earn 'clutch player' status — penalty FTs for falling short.
- [Drill one on one cutthroat live](drill-one-on-one-cutthroat-live.md) — Competitive 1-on-1 cutthroat drill to 21 with make-it/take-it rule after 3 points — tests all live-ball moves in a full game-like competitive setting.
- [Drill fade shot off screen](drill-fade-shot-off-screen.md) — Progressive fade shot workout (25, 50, 100 reps) from 15–20 feet: shooter sets up under basket, uses screener, and catches a pass on the fade for a midrange jump shot.
- [Drill dribble fade off screen](drill-dribble-fade-off-screen.md) — Dribble fade drill (25 reps): catcher receives on the wing off a screen, defender closes out high, cutter attacks the baseline with a dribble for any scoring opportunity.
- [Drill dribble fade shots](drill-dribble-fade-shots.md) — Progressive shooting workout series (25–100 reps) — catch off screen on wing, read high-angle closeout, attack baseline with dribble fade for any scoring opportunity.
- [Drill fill shots off screen](drill-fill-shots-off-screen.md) — Progressive catch-and-shoot wing drill (25–100 reps) — use screen, fill to wing, shoot 15–20 ft catch-and-shoot when defender is beaten.
- [Drill dribble fill shots](drill-dribble-fill-shots.md) — Progressive shooting workout (25–100 reps) — catch off screen, read trailing/low-side closeout, attack middle of paint with dribble fill for any scoring opportunity.
- [Drill curl shots off screen](drill-curl-shots-off-screen.md) — Progressive curl shot workout (25–100 reps) — use screen, curl to elbow area (10–15 ft), catch-and-shoot when defender is high or chasing.
- [Drill dribble curl shots](drill-dribble-curl-shots.md) — Progressive dribble curl workout (25–100 reps) — defender trails directly behind on curl cut, so cutter continues into paint with a dribble curl for any scoring opportunity.
- [Drill 400 shots off screen](drill-400-shots-off-screen.md) — Comprehensive 400+ shot workout combining all off-screen shooting and live-ball attacking moves — fade, fill, curl, dribble fade, dribble fill, dribble curl — in one elite training session.
- [Drill shots a day club](drill-shots-a-day-club.md) — Shots-a-Day Club: structured daily shooting workouts (300+ and 500+ shots) using shot fakes, rip steps, and free throws for dedicated skill development.
- [Drill off season challenge workouts](drill-off-season-challenge-workouts.md) — Off-season shooting challenge workouts: 10,000 / 15,000 / 20,000 total game-shot goals and 1,000–4,000 three-point makes challenges with tracking charts.
- [Drill shoot the pyramid](drill-shoot-the-pyramid.md) — Shoot the Pyramid game: make 6-5-4-3-2 consecutive shots in descending order with FT penalty for misses — builds pressure shooting and competitive focus.
- [Drill spot shot workout](drill-spot-shot-workout.md) — Solo full-speed spot shot workout series — throw-to-self, sprint to ball, square up and shoot; scalable from 50 to 100+ shots with free-throw sets between rounds.
- [Drill follow the leader shooting workouts](drill-follow-the-leader-shooting-workouts.md) — Follow-the-Leader group shooting workout series — players mirror each other's exact shot (spot shots, 3PT, combo moves, rip steps, shot fakes, open-court dribble moves) in alternating-rep format.
- [Drill favorite spot shooting workouts](drill-favorite-spot-shooting-workouts.md) — Self-selected favorite spot shooting workouts — player picks 3 strongest spots and must reach a make quota (10/20/30) per spot; confidence-building and make-based accountability.
- [Drill weakest spot shooting workouts](drill-weakest-spot-shooting-workouts.md) — Self-selected weakest spot shooting workouts — player picks 3 hardest spots and must reach a make quota (10/20/30) per spot; forces players to confront and improve their lowest-percentage areas.
- [Drill wing to top three point shooting](drill-wing-to-top-three-point-shooting.md) — Wing-to-Top Three-Point Shooting (Workout #11-16): player moves wing→top→wing taking 10 three-point shots per set, both sides, game speed.
- [Drill wing to top combination live ball move shooting](drill-wing-to-top-combination-live-ball-move-shooting.md) — Wing-to-Top Combo Live-Ball Move Shooting (Workout #11-17): two-foot stop catch beyond arc, execute combination live-ball move, shoot; wing→top→wing both sides.
- [Drill wing to top rip step live ball move shooting](drill-wing-to-top-rip-step-live-ball-move-shooting.md) — Wing-to-Top Rip Step Live-Ball Move Shooting (Workout #11-18): two-foot stop beyond arc, rip step live-ball move, shoot; wing→top→wing both sides game speed.
- [Drill wing to top shot fake live ball move shooting](drill-wing-to-top-shot-fake-live-ball-move-shooting.md) — Wing-to-Top Shot Fake (SF) Live-Ball Move Shooting (Workout #11-19): two-foot stop beyond arc, shot fake live-ball move, shoot; wing→top→wing both sides game speed.
- [Drill back squat](drill-back-squat.md) — Barbell back squat for basketball lower-extremity strength: execution, primary muscles (quads, glutes, hamstrings), and coaching cues for safe technique.
- [Drill contralateral kick](drill-contralateral-kick.md) — Unilateral ankle proprioception drill: balance on the injured leg while kicking the opposite leg against a resistance band in multiple planes.
- [Drill mat walk](drill-mat-walk.md) — Tightrope-style mat walk drill for knee rehabilitation — builds dynamic balance during forward movement, simulating direction changes and cuts on court.
- [Drill ytw shoulder](drill-ytw-shoulder.md) — YTW Physioball exercise: three-position scapular stabilizer strengthening drill for basketball players to improve shoulder firing patterns for shooting, defending, and blocking.
- [Drill cheerleader resistance band](drill-cheerleader-resistance-band.md) — Cheerleader resistance band exercise: multi-directional arm pattern with a band to strengthen scapular stabilizers and rotator cuff for shooting and defending.
- [Drill back squat basketball](drill-back-squat-basketball.md) — The barbell back squat for basketball — primary lower-extremity strength exercise targeting quads, glutes, hamstrings, and core for jumping and force production.
- [Exercise front squat](exercise-front-squat.md) — Front Squat — barbell leg strength exercise emphasizing quadriceps, glutes, and hamstrings for basketball acceleration, jumping, and deceleration.
- [Exercise deadlift](exercise-deadlift.md) — Deadlift — multi-joint barbell exercise building posterior chain strength for basketball force output, jumping, layups, boxing out, and rebounding.
- [Exercise romanian deadlift](exercise-romanian-deadlift.md) — Romanian Deadlift (RDL) — hip-hinge exercise building hamstring and glute strength for running, jumping, deceleration, cutting, and injury prevention.
- [Exercise hip thrust](exercise-hip-thrust.md) — Hip Thrust — barbell glute exercise building horizontal/vertical propulsion, safe landing mechanics, deceleration, and cutting ability for basketball.
- [Exercise reverse lunge](exercise-reverse-lunge.md) — Reverse Lunge — unilateral leg exercise building quad/glute strength, balance, and proprioception for basketball acceleration, jumping, and direction changes.
- [Exercise reverse step down from box](exercise-reverse-step-down-from-box.md) — Reverse Step-Down From Box — single-leg strength and proprioception exercise for basketball running, jumping, layups, cutting, and contact stability.
- [Exercise band backward walk](exercise-band-backward-walk.md) — Band Backward Walk — partner-resisted backward walk developing quadriceps/glute strength endurance for basketball defense, acceleration, and deceleration.
- [Exercise band lateral walk](exercise-band-lateral-walk.md) — Band Lateral Walk — miniband lateral movement exercise building hip abductor strength for basketball defensive slides, direction changes, and driving lanes.
- [Exercise calf pop up](exercise-calf-pop-up.md) — Calf Pop-Up — explosive calf raise exercise building gastrocnemius/soleus/Achilles tendon strength for jumping height, second-jump ability, and rebounding.
- [Drill banana](drill-banana.md) — Banana hold — isometric core flexion exercise building inner core trunk stability for jumping, rebounding, and contact resistance.
- [Drill supine basketball core pass](drill-supine-basketball-core-pass.md) — Supine basketball core pass — core flexion drill using a basketball passed hand-to-foot to build anterior chain strength and trunk stability.
- [Drill back extension](drill-back-extension.md) — Back extension on hyperextension machine — posterior chain and core extension exercise for jumping power and defensive upper-body posture.
- [Drill bird dog](drill-bird-dog.md) — Quadruped arm and leg lift (Bird Dog) — core extension stability exercise for spinal stability, resisting box-out contact, and defensive ground-holding.
- [Drill pallof press](drill-pallof-press.md) — Horizontal Cable Core (Pallof) Press — anti-rotation core exercise building stability for ball security, defensive positioning, and rebound battles.
- [Drill landmine trunk rotation](drill-landmine-trunk-rotation.md) — Landmine trunk rotation — rotational core power exercise using a barbell to build trunk strength for driving, rebounding, and defensive rotation.
- [Drill lateral plank](drill-lateral-plank.md) — Lateral plank — lateral core stability exercise building hip and trunk strength for jumping power, balance, and physical play against bigger opponents.
- [Drill overhead cable core press](drill-overhead-cable-core-press.md) — Overhead cable core press — lateral flexion anti-rotation exercise building shoulder and oblique stability for reaching, rebounding, and shooting.
- [Drill pull up basketball](drill-pull-up-basketball.md) — Pull-up exercise for basketball: develops upper-back strength for rebounding, running, and defending — with band-assisted and grip variations.
- [Drill inverted row basketball](drill-inverted-row-basketball.md) — Inverted row exercise for basketball: posterior deltoid and upper-back developer supporting shooting, defense, and body control — with tabletop and TRX variations.
- [Drill lat pull down basketball](drill-lat-pull-down-basketball.md) — Lat pull-down machine exercise for basketball: variable-resistance upper-back developer for running, rebounding, injury prevention, and paint physicality.
- [Drill single arm dumbbell row basketball](drill-single-arm-dumbbell-row-basketball.md) — Single-arm dumbbell row for basketball: unilateral posterior deltoid and lat developer addressing strength imbalances for shooting, rebounding, and non-dominant hand use.
- [Drill seated row basketball](drill-seated-row-basketball.md) — Seated cable row for basketball: builds latissimus dorsi and shoulder girdle stability for posture, injury prevention, paint physicality, and scoring through contact.
- [Drill barbell bent over row basketball](drill-barbell-bent-over-row-basketball.md) — Barbell bent-over row for basketball: advanced free-weight pulling exercise building upper and lower back strength for athletic position, running, and court physicality.
- [Drill kettlebell high pull basketball](drill-kettlebell-high-pull-basketball.md) — Kettlebell high pull for basketball: explosive multi-joint pulling exercise developing shoulder power and fast-twitch activation for jumping and rebounding.
- [Drill renegade row basketball](drill-renegade-row-basketball.md) — Renegade row for basketball: advanced push-pull plank exercise building shoulder stability, core anti-rotation strength, and upper-body balance for passing, shooting, and rebounding.
- [Drill push up basketball](drill-push-up-basketball.md) — Basketball-specific push-up drill with knee and platform variations — builds chest, shoulder, and triceps strength for passing, defending, and screening.
- [Drill bench press basketball](drill-bench-press-basketball.md) — Barbell bench press for basketball players — builds chest and shoulder strength for post play, passing power, and absorbing contact under the basket.
- [Drill overhead press basketball](drill-overhead-press-basketball.md) — Standing overhead barbell press — builds deltoid and shoulder strength critical for shooting, rebounding, and overhead actions in basketball.
- [Drill single arm band press basketball](drill-single-arm-band-press-basketball.md) — Single-arm elastic band press in staggered stance — builds unilateral chest/shoulder strength for passing and dribbling without gym equipment.
- [Drill incline barbell press basketball](drill-incline-barbell-press-basketball.md) — Incline barbell press at 45°+ — targets upper chest and anterior deltoid for chest-pass force and rebounding position strength.
- [Drill single arm landmine press basketball](drill-single-arm-landmine-press-basketball.md) — Single-arm landmine press in defensive stance — mimics layup/dunk overhead extension; builds unilateral shoulder strength for finishing and rebounding.
- [Drill close grip bench press basketball](drill-close-grip-bench-press-basketball.md) — Close-grip bench press — shifts emphasis to triceps for explosive chest-pass strength, shot-blocking position, and ball-protection strength.
- [Drill kettlebell swing](drill-kettlebell-swing.md) — Kettlebell swing: introductory hip-thrust and triple-extension drill for basketball explosive power, targeting glutes, hamstrings, quads, and back.
- [Drill snatch pull hang](drill-snatch-pull-hang.md) — Snatch pull from hang position: barbell explosive pull developing vertical jump power and on-court explosiveness; prerequisite to the full power snatch.
- [Drill clean pull hang](drill-clean-pull-hang.md) — Clean pull from hang position: barbell explosive pull with narrow grip building jumping/acceleration force; prerequisite to the full power clean.
- [Drill power snatch hang](drill-power-snatch-hang.md) — Power snatch from hang position: advanced Olympic lift developing explosive total-body power, shoulder stability, and core strength with basketball-specific application.
- [Drill power snatch floor](drill-power-snatch-floor.md) — Power snatch from floor: most advanced snatch variation — full range pull from floor requires maximum joint mobility and teaches explosive acceleration from a dead stop.
- [Drill power clean hang](drill-power-clean-hang.md) — Power clean from hang position: advanced Olympic lift for total-body explosive power, jump height, acceleration, and contact stability in the air.
- [Drill tuck jump](drill-tuck-jump.md) — Tuck jump plyometric: bilateral explosive jump with knee tuck — builds vertical leap, reactive strength, and rebound ability for all positions.
- [Drill single leg hurdle jump](drill-single-leg-hurdle-jump.md) — Single-leg hurdle jump plyometric: unilateral explosive hurdle jumps developing single-leg power for first-step quickness, cutting, and one-leg take-off layups.
- [Drill depth jump into jump shot](drill-depth-jump-into-jump-shot.md) — Depth jump into jump shot — step off a box (12-30 in.), land with both feet, immediately simulate a jump shot; trains reactive power and game-specific vertical.
- [Drill multiple box jump](drill-multiple-box-jump.md) — Multiple-box jump plyometric — consecutive box-to-floor-to-box jumps (2-4 boxes, 12-30 in.) building reactive floor quickness for rebounds, loose balls, and direction changes.
- [Drill skater hop](drill-skater-hop.md) — Skater hop plyometric — lateral single-leg hops simulating defensive slides and quick cuts; builds lateral hip explosiveness and knee injury prevention.
- [Drill split jump into run](drill-split-jump-into-run.md) — Split jump into run plyometric — split squat jump followed by immediate sprint; develops first-step quickness and fast-break acceleration from a rebound landing position.
- [Drill pivot step medicine ball chest pass](drill-pivot-step-medicine-ball-chest-pass.md) — Pivot step to medicine ball chest pass — upper-body plyometric combining a footwork pivot with an explosive chest pass; trains quick jab step and passing power.
- [Drill medicine ball slam vertical jump](drill-medicine-ball-slam-vertical-jump.md) — Medicine ball slam into vertical jump — overhead slam followed by instant max-effort vertical jump; builds total-body power for driving, dunking, and rebounding.
- [Drill medicine ball push up](drill-medicine-ball-push-up.md) — Medicine ball push-up plyometric — explosive push-up transitioning hands to/from a medicine ball; builds upper-body power for passing, rebounding, and boxing out.
- [Drill single leg stance balance](drill-single-leg-stance-balance.md) — Single-leg stance ankle balance drill — stand on affected leg with slight knee bend; foundational rehabilitation and proprioception exercise for ankle sprains and general stability.
- [Drill rocker board balance](drill-rocker-board-balance.md) — Ankle balance drill on rocker board or BOSU — minisquat on unstable surface builds ankle/quad stability for explosiveness and injury prevention.
- [Drill seated physioball perturbation](drill-seated-physioball-perturbation.md) — Seated ankle proprioception drill using a Physioball — acute-phase rehabilitation exercise restoring ankle neuromuscular control after sprain.
- [Drill hopping proprioception](drill-hopping-proprioception.md) — Progressive hopping drill building lower-extremity propulsion, deceleration ability, and proprioception — directly transfers to rebounding and floor reaction speed.
- [Drill contralateral kick balance](drill-contralateral-kick-balance.md) — Unilateral balance drill with resistance band kicks — trains single-leg proprioception and ankle stability critical for layups, off-balance shots, and loose ball pursuit.
- [Drill resistive ankle motion](drill-resistive-ankle-motion.md) — Seated resistance band ankle strengthening drill covering full range of motion — targets the muscles most responsible for preventing ankle sprains.
- [Drill standing heel raise](drill-standing-heel-raise.md) — Standing heel raise — fundamental ankle strengthening exercise building calf plantar flexion power for running, jumping, and explosive court movements.
- [Drill band lateral walk](drill-band-lateral-walk.md) — Resistance band lateral walk in minisquat — builds lateral ankle stability, hip abductor strength, and athletic base for cutting and driving defenders.
- [Drill mat walk knee rehab](drill-mat-walk-knee-rehab.md) — Tightrope mat walk drill for knee rehabilitation — builds dynamic balance and ankle/lower-extremity stability during movement essential for cutting and driving.
- [Drill single leg stance unstable surface](drill-single-leg-stance-unstable-surface.md) — Single-leg stance on BOSU/foam pad — knee rehab drill building unilateral quad strength, knee/ankle stability, and single-leg power for driving and rebounding.
- [Drill eccentric leg press](drill-eccentric-leg-press.md) — Eccentric leg press — sub-bodyweight slow-lowering exercise for jumper's knee rehab; rebuilds patellar tendon loading capacity and jump landing strength.
- [Drill body weight squat knee rehab](drill-body-weight-squat-knee-rehab.md) — Body-weight squat for jumper's knee rehabilitation — restores bilateral lower-extremity strength and stability as a baseline for progressive loading.
- [Drill step down knee rehab](drill-step-down-knee-rehab.md) — Step-down from plyometric box — eccentric quad strengthening drill for jumper's knee rehab and a readiness-to-run test for returning players.
- [Drill box jump knee rehab](drill-box-jump-knee-rehab.md) — Box jump for knee rehabilitation — plyometric reintroduction exercise that outputs high power with reduced landing impact forces, restoring court explosiveness safely.
- [Drill posterior capsule stretch](drill-posterior-capsule-stretch.md) — Posterior capsule stretch restoring shoulder flexibility for increased shooting and defending range of motion.
- [Drill latissimus dorsi stretch](drill-latissimus-dorsi-stretch.md) — Latissimus dorsi stretch restoring back and shoulder flexibility for improved shooting and defending range of motion.
- [Drill pectoralis stretch](drill-pectoralis-stretch.md) — Pectoralis stretch in a corner or doorway restoring chest and shoulder flexibility for shooting and defending.
- [Drill sleeper stretch](drill-sleeper-stretch.md) — Side-lying sleeper stretch targeting the rotator cuff and posterior deltoid to improve shoulder internal rotation range of motion.
- [Drill thoracic spine mobility](drill-thoracic-spine-mobility.md) — Thoracic spine rotation drill in quadruped position to restore upper-back and shoulder mobility for shooting and defending.
- [Drill ytw shoulder strengthening](drill-ytw-shoulder-strengthening.md) — YTW exercise on a Physioball — three-position scapular stabilizer strengthening drill for shooting, defending, and blocking.
- [Drill side lying shoulder external rotation](drill-side-lying-shoulder-external-rotation.md) — Side-lying rotator cuff external rotation exercise to strengthen infraspinatus and teres minor for shooting, defending, and blocking.
- [Drill cheerleader shoulder strengthening](drill-cheerleader-shoulder-strengthening.md) — Resistance band 'Cheerleader' exercise — multi-directional scapular stabilizer strengthening for shooting, defending, and blocking.
- [Drill overhead press shoulder](drill-overhead-press-shoulder.md) — Overhead press with barbell or dumbbells strengthening the rotator cuff and deltoids to improve shooting, defending, and blocking.
- [Drill overhead medicine ball toss](drill-overhead-medicine-ball-toss.md) — Overhead medicine ball wall toss — plyometric shoulder strengthening to increase power for shooting and rebounding.
- [Drill band squat](drill-band-squat.md) — Resistance band squat with elastic band below knees to strengthen lateral hips and correct dynamic valgus (ligament dominance ACL pattern).
- [Drill band defensive slide](drill-band-defensive-slide.md) — Resistance band defensive slide — lateral hip strengthening exercise that mimics on-court defensive footwork while correcting dynamic valgus.
- [Drill side lying clam](drill-side-lying-clam.md) — Side-lying clam exercise with resistance band to develop gluteal and hip external rotator strength for ACL injury prevention.
- [Drill physioball hamstring curl](drill-physioball-hamstring-curl.md) — Physioball hamstring curl in bridge position to strengthen the posterior chain and correct quadriceps dominance ACL risk pattern.
- [Drill shooting hand form shooting](drill-shooting-hand-form-shooting.md) — One-handed form shooting drill that isolates shooting-arm alignment, starting 2 feet from the basket and progressing back a half-step at a time.
- [Drill balance hand form shooting](drill-balance-hand-form-shooting.md) — Two-hand form shooting drill that adds the balance hand to the shooting-hand drill, verifying that balance hand placement does not disrupt elbow alignment.
- [Drill freeze follow through](drill-freeze-follow-through.md) — Shooting drill where players hold their follow-through until the ball hits the floor to build muscle memory and allow coach feedback.
- [Drill eggs on the rim](drill-eggs-on-the-rim.md) — Visualization drill where shooters imagine eggs on the rim to promote high arch, proper follow-through, and center-basket targeting.
- [Drill free shot swish](drill-free-shot-swish.md) — Competitive 1-on-1 free-throw drill awarding 2 pts for a swish, 1 for a make, −1 for a miss; play to 11 win-by-2.
- [Drill free shot 3 25](drill-free-shot-3-25.md) — Team free-throw drill: make 25 shots before 3 misses; each miss = a sprint. Builds mental toughness and team accountability.
- [Drill free shot five balance hand](drill-free-shot-five-balance-hand.md) — Multi-skill drill combining free-shot shooting (freeze finish) with weak-hand layups and weak-hand dribbling in one efficient sequence.
- [Drill free shot make two sprint](drill-free-shot-make-two-sprint.md) — Conditioning free-throw drill: make 2 consecutive shots, sprint to baseline and back; miss = immediate sprint. Reach 20 total makes.
- [Drill partner shooting midrange](drill-partner-shooting-midrange.md) — Two-player catch-and-shoot midrange drill from 7 spots; passer delivers from under basket, shooter uses one-two step mechanics and freezes follow-through.
- [Drill one dribble two dribble pull up](drill-one-dribble-two-dribble-pull-up.md) — Fundamental pull-up jump shot drills using one or two dribbles, going both directions with each foot as the pivot, building two-way pull-up competency.
- [Shooting hand form shooting drill](shooting-hand-form-shooting-drill.md) — One-handed form shooting drill to isolate elbow alignment and build proper shooting mechanics from close range outward.
- [Balance hand form shooting drill](balance-hand-form-shooting-drill.md) — Two-handed close-range form shooting drill that maintains elbow alignment while adding the balance hand to the shot.
- [Drill spinouts midrange](drill-spinouts-midrange.md) — Solo catch-and-shoot drill simulating game catches: spin ball to self, one-two step into jump shot from 7 midrange spots.
- [Drill partner shooting](drill-partner-shooting.md) — Two-player catch-and-shoot drill from 7 midrange spots with a live passer; builds rhythm, communication, and consistent follow-through.
- [Drill closeout shooting](drill-closeout-shooting.md) — Partner catch-and-shoot drill with live defensive closeout; trains shooter to stay low and shoot over pressure without dipping the ball.
- [Drill triangle passing shooting](drill-triangle-passing-shooting.md) — High-rep group shooting drill in a triangle formation (rebounder under hoop, passers at elbow, shooters on baseline) simulating angled game passes.
- [Drill transition jump shot](drill-transition-jump-shot.md) — Group drill teaching players to transition from a full-speed sprint to a balanced one-two step jump shot, with passer timing the pass to the stride.
- [Drill stop and pop](drill-stop-and-pop.md) — Individual or team pull-up jump shot drill off the dribble: speed dribble up court, stop on a dime, shoot a 12–15 ft jump shot with each hand.
- [Drill pull up jump shot](drill-pull-up-jump-shot.md) — One- and two-dribble pull-up drills building the straight-on pull-up jump shot with both hands and both pivot feet.
- [Bank shot drills](bank-shot-drills.md) — Three progressive bank shot drills: form shooting at 45°, close-to-midrange spinouts, under-basket turnaround, and pull-up off the dribble.
- [Drill show and go closeout 1on1](drill-show-and-go-closeout-1on1.md) — Competitive 1-on-1-on-1 closeout drill developing show-and-go reads, scoring mindset, and defender closeout recognition from seven shooting spots and on the move.
- [Drill jab step progression](drill-jab-step-progression.md) — Progressive jab step drill series: stationary to on-the-move, shooting foot to nonshooting foot, with live defender closeout reads and competitive scoring.
- [Drill step back progression](drill-step-back-progression.md) — Step-back drill progression: footwork-first approach from top of key through wing on-the-move catches, covering weak-side, strong-side, and the step-back-rise-up-and-go counter.
- [Drill around the world spinouts](drill-around-the-world-spinouts.md) — Around-the-world spinout shooting drill — practice catch-and-shoot footwork along the full 3-point arc using self-pass spinouts.
- [Drill spinouts to from baseline](drill-spinouts-to-from-baseline.md) — Spinout drill simulating down-screen and inbounds-screen passes from both top and baseline angles — catch-and-shoot off varied angles.
- [Drill left to right v cut](drill-left-to-right-v-cut.md) — Team shooting drill: shooter makes a V-cut off imaginary defender, receives a pass in rhythm, and fires a catch-and-shoot with proper footwork.
- [Drill baseline shooting](drill-baseline-shooting.md) — Team shooting drill running from elbow to elbow along the baseline — angle cuts, inside-foot plant, heel-to-toe stepping, catch-and-shoot in rhythm.
- [Drill sideline shooting](drill-sideline-shooting.md) — Wing-to-wing V-cut shooting drill from two lines at free-throw line extended — players alternate cutting and catching for balanced catch-and-shoot reps.

## Plays
- [Play guard oriented attack](play-guard-oriented-attack.md) — Guard-Oriented Attack from Winning Basketball Fundamentals — 5-out set using guard V-cuts, high-post screening, and simultaneous down screens to free guards for shots off PnR or DHO.
- [Play forward oriented attack](play-forward-oriented-attack.md) — Forward-Oriented Attack from Winning Basketball Fundamentals — wing-player feature set using hand-offs, center screens, post-ups, split action, and staggered double screens.
- [Play power down attack](play-power-down-attack.md) — Power Down Attack from Winning Basketball Fundamentals — 1-4 box set low-post entry system using down screens, split action, and ball reversal to feed a dominant center.
- [Play power cross attack](play-power-cross-attack.md) — Power Cross Attack from Winning Basketball Fundamentals — screen-the-screener low-post entry from a 2-guard front with cross screens, down screens, and indirect post feed to a dominant center.
- [Play three point x out slob](play-three-point-x-out-slob.md) — Three-Point X-Out SLOB — pick-the-picker screening action frees two shooters for catch-and-shoot 3PT attempts when down 3 [S13, p.247]
- [Play x out single double](play-x-out-single-double.md) — X-Out Into Single-Double SLOB — staggered double screen frees a shooter to the top of the key when down 3 points [S13, p.248]
- [Play inside pick the picker blob](play-inside-pick-the-picker-blob.md) — Inside Pick-the-Picker BLOB — baseline OOB play using a double-stagger decoy then pick-the-picker to free the post for a layup [S13, pp.248-249]
- [Play box cross 2 blob](play-box-cross-2-blob.md) — Box Cross 2 BLOB — simple box-set baseline play using a cross screen and decoy to free a cutter for a lob or layup [S13, pp.249-250]
- [Play line blob](play-line-blob.md) — Line BLOB — the most adaptable baseline inbounds alignment; four sequential cutters beat full-court pressure and get ball to PG [S13, p.251]
- [Play lob blob](play-lob-blob.md) — Lob BLOB — frontcourt baseline inbounds play using deception (fake up screen) and a cross screen to free a post player for a lob finish [S13, p.252]
- [Play versus 1 3 1](play-versus-1-3-1.md) — Versus 1-3-1 — misdirection guard-to-forward set using ball reversal, low-block screen, and lob to attack a 1-3-1 half-court zone [S13, pp.253-254]
- [Play versus box and one](play-versus-box-and-one.md) — Versus Box-and-One — modified LA offense using screening to occupy zone defenders and create a passing triangle for open shots [S13, pp.254-255]
- [Play versus triangle and two](play-versus-triangle-and-two.md) — Versus Triangle-and-Two — guards dive to blocks, creating a 3-on-2+ overload for unguarded perimeter players; patience and rebounding are keys [S13, pp.255-256]
- [Play san antonio early offense corner fill](play-san-antonio-early-offense-corner-fill.md) — San Antonio Spurs (Popovich) early offense — Corner Fill action: high-low twin towers system with three options including post feed, high-low pass, and ball reversal to weak-side post.
- [Play san antonio guard through](play-san-antonio-guard-through.md) — San Antonio Spurs early offense — Guard Through, Through with Cross Screen, and High Post Dive Action: Popovich's secondary early-offense reads flowing from the corner fill structure.
- [Play detroit step up flare](play-detroit-step-up-flare.md) — Detroit Pistons step-up PnR with flare: 3 drives off 2's step-up screen; if stopped, 4 back-screens 2 for skip-pass flare, 5 down-screens for 1 — multiple outlet options [S14, pp.27-29]
- [Play detroit double pnr series](play-detroit-double-pnr-series.md) — Detroit Pistons double PnR series (Collins/Gentry): stacked double PnR and staggered double PnR — 3 drives off big who rolls, second big pops — multiple ball-side and weak-side options [S14, pp.31]
- [Play minnesota triple pnr](play-minnesota-triple-pnr.md) — Minnesota Timberwolves triple pick-and-roll (Flip Saunders): double stack into single PnR, cleared weak side — Brandon feeds Garnett in post or reverses to swing options [S14, pp.37]
- [Play charlotte pnr back screen](play-charlotte-pnr-back-screen.md) — Charlotte Hornets PnR with back screen (Paul Silas): 1-5 wing PnR initiates, 2 back-screens for 5 who crosses lane to post up — two post-up target variations [S14, pp.33]
- [Play orlando angled pnr](play-orlando-angled-pnr.md) — Orlando Magic angled wing PnR (Chuck Daly/Doc Rivers): 45-degree angle PnR with weak-side staggered screens — attacks teams that force sideline or trap; four scoring options [S14, pp.33-36]
- [Play miami pnr baseline screening](play-miami-pnr-baseline-screening.md) — Miami Heat PnR into baseline screening action (Pat Riley): wing PnR with triple weak-side stack — 5 rolls to down-screen for 2 while 4 down-screens for 3; three scoring options [S14, pp.39]
- [Play new jersey loop action](play-new-jersey-loop-action.md) — NBA Loop action — staggered screens by 4 and 5 free the best shooter (2) to the top or wing — New Jersey Nets (Calipari) and Milwaukee Bucks (Karl) variations with post-up continuity [S14, pp.41-43]
- [Play philadelphia baseline screening](play-philadelphia-baseline-screening.md) — Philadelphia 76ers baseline screening plays (Larry Brown): staggered screens free Allen Iverson (2) — lob option, handoff drive, flare-and-isolation, and flare-to-PnR variations [S14, pp.44-46]
- [Play celtics x action](play-celtics-x-action.md) — Boston Celtics 1-4 high 'X Action' — cutting off elbows, down screen, back screen, and 1-5 PnR with multiple lob/punch/spot-up reads (Rick Pitino system)
- [Play celtics post drop](play-celtics-post-drop.md) — Boston Celtics 'Post-Drop' from 1-4 high — hard backdoor cut to post-up, down-screen option, and back-screen lob option for the power forward (Rick Pitino)
- [Play utah jazz ucla action](play-utah-jazz-ucla-action.md) — Utah Jazz 1-4 high UCLA Action (Jerry Sloan) — wing pass + UCLA cut off elbow, staggered screens, back screen for post, pick-the-picker, and dribble entry variants
- [Play knicks zipper baseline triple](play-knicks-zipper-baseline-triple.md) — NY Knicks 'Zipper-to-Baseline Triple' — zipper screen frees the 2 at top, PG runs triple baseline staggered screens, with 1-on-1 and elbow PnR alternatives (Jeff Van Gundy, 1999 NBA Finals)
- [Play hawks zipper cross screen](play-hawks-zipper-cross-screen.md) — Atlanta Hawks 'Zipper-to-Cross Screen' — 5-3 zipper followed by back screen lob, cross screen for the 5, and pick-the-picker continuity (Lenny Wilkens / Dikembe Mutombo post focus)
- [Play minnesota hawk combination](play-minnesota-hawk-combination.md) — Minnesota Timberwolves 'Hawk Combination' — moving Hawk back screen, weak-side double screen, and wing PnR for Garnett/Brandon, with counter double-screen continuity (Flip Saunders)
- [Play indiana box high x](play-indiana-box-high-x.md) — Indiana Pacers 'Box Set High X' — PF and C cross in the high post, one posts the block, the other sets a down screen for the 2, creating post + perimeter opportunities (Larry Bird / Reggie Miller / Rik Smits)
- [Play motion offense cross screen](play-cross-screen.md) — Motion Offense cross-screen + parallel double screen play from a box set — PG dribbles left wing, triggering cross screen for post, then screener cuts high off double screen for open catch-and-shoot.
- [Play motion offense up screen](play-up-screen.md) — Motion Offense 'Up Screen' play from a box set — back screen frees a post player, with down screen continuity creating multiple reads for the PG from a corner elbow receiver.
- [Play motion offense diagonal screen](play-diagonal-screen.md) — Motion Offense 'Diagonal Screen' play — diagonal screen frees guard to post up, followed by screen-the-screener continuity giving the PG four passing options.
- [Play motion offense pick and roll](play-pick-and-roll-layered.md) — Motion Offense 'Pick-and-Roll' box set play — high-post rub cut posts up a guard, side screen (PnR) for PG, followed by perpendicular double-screen baseline for the guard.
- [Play continuity pass screen away](play-pass-and-screen-away.md) — Continuity offense 'Pass and Screen Away' set: five options from the 2-3 high-post formation — high-post catch, backdoor, down screen, roll, and reverse-dribble continuity.
- [Play continuity pass cut away](play-pass-and-cut-away.md) — Continuity 'Pass and Cut Away' set: both perimeter players cut away from the ball after the high-post entry, filling all four perimeter spots and eliminating strong/weak side.
- [Play continuity high split](play-high-split-action.md) — Continuity 'Pass and Follow the Ball (High Split)': passer follows the high-post entry, triggering a split with five secondary options — pick-and-roll, backdoor, pop-out, and back-screen.
- [Play continuity reverse dribble](play-reverse-dribble-options.md) — Continuity reverse dribble entry options: when no pass is available, the ball handler initiates with a reverse dribble triggering backdoor cuts, screens, hand-offs, PnR, and double-screen reads.
- [Play continuity chin](play-chin-series.md) — Continuity 'Chin' action: high-post back-pick on the weak side — two base options plus the Chin Pass to Strong Side (Flare Action) with simultaneous down screens and flare screens.
- [Play continuity high pick sets](play-high-pick-series.md) — Continuity 'Sets Out of the High Pick': high on-ball screen for PG from the 5, with double-screen continuity, hand-off DHO, and PnR reads — two option trees.
- [Blob stack zone variant](blob-stack-zone-variant.md) — BLOB vs 2-3 zone (stack ball-side): shooter drags wing defender to corner while center screens middle, creating gap for post midrange or corner 3.
- [Blob 4 low flex updated](blob-4-low-flex-updated.md) — BLOB man-to-man play from 4-low formation: lob inbound to top, flex screen for post layup, screen-the-screener pin down for best shooter catch-and-shoot.
- [Blob box gate updated](blob-box-gate-updated.md) — BLOB man play from box: best shooter back-screens for center's layup, then sprints through a gate screen for wing catch-and-shoot; post cross-screen as tertiary option.
- [Blob flip updated](blob-flip-updated.md) — BLOB man box play: guards flash to corners, cross-screen frees two post players attacking the rim simultaneously; PG reads and passes to the open layup.
- [Blob stack double updated](blob-stack-double-updated.md) — BLOB man-to-man stack play: ball reversal through two passes, PG fake dribble draws defense, staggered double screen frees best shooter for wing shot.
- [Blob stack man spread](blob-stack-man-spread.md) — Simple youth BLOB man-to-man from stack: first two players blast to corner and block, third player in line steps in open for near-basket shot; 5 is safety.
- [Blob two inside updated](blob-two-inside-updated.md) — BLOB man box play using screen-the-screener to feed either post player at the rim; guards occupy perimeter defenders; reset option available.
- [Blob yo yo updated](blob-yo-yo-updated.md) — Simple box BLOB: guards set simultaneous up-screens for two post players who explode to the basket for layups; guard wing cut as safety valve.
- [Set 23 flare updated](set-23-flare-updated.md) — Set play vs 2-3 zone from 1-3-1: extended ball movement draws zone defenders, then a quick flare screen from the 5 frees the best shooter for an open three-pointer.
- [Set 32 lob updated](set-32-lob-updated.md) — Set play vs 2-3 zone from 3-out 2-in: overload one side, shift the zone, then screen the weak-side low defender for an athletic player's backdoor lob finish.
- [Play baseline swing](play-baseline-swing.md) — 2-3 zone play: baseline cut off post screen forces low defender choice — mid-range or three-point shot for shooter in corner.
- [Play doubles](play-doubles.md) — Man-to-man quick hitter from 1-4 high: best shooter cuts off a double screen for an open perimeter shot.
- [Play flare overload](play-flare-overload.md) — 2-3 zone play from 1-3-1: on-ball screen and position swaps force 1 defender to cover 3 perimeter players for an open three.
- [Play low split](play-low-split.md) — 2-3 zone play from 1-3-1: dual post flashes into the heart of the zone for a layup, close shot, or drawn foul.
- [Play pick overload](play-pick-overload.md) — 2-3 zone play from 1-3-1: on-ball screen drives the point guard, overloading one side 3v2 for an open wing or corner three.
- [Play skipper](play-skipper.md) — 2-3 zone quick hitter from 1-3-1: post screens the back-side zone defender, shooter slides to corner for skip pass three.
- [Play step up](play-step-up.md) — 2-3 zone surprise play from 1-3-1: step-up screen on wing triggers baseline drive, forced rotation opens layup or wing three.
- [Play swinger](play-swinger.md) — Man-to-man set play from 1-3-1: blindside PnR for the point guard at the top of the key with three read-based scoring options.
- [Play 1 4 quick floppy](play-1-4-quick-floppy.md) — Man-to-man set play from 1-4 high: both guards simultaneously cut off post screens (floppy action) for immediate perimeter looks or post duck-ins.
- [Play back screen post](play-back-screen-post.md) — Man-to-man set play from 3-out 2-in: PG dribbles off staggered screen, triggering back screen to free the post for a layup or deep post; staggered screen for shooter as secondary.
- [Play black](play-black.md) — Man-to-man quick hitter from 5-out: corner step-up screen triggers wing baseline drive, with opposite post flash for layup or perimeter kick-out.
- [Play drive hammer](play-drive-hammer.md) — Box set half-court play: PnR drives to rim with hammer screen on corner guard and two corner passing options.
- [Play flex warrior](play-flex-warrior.md) — Horns set half-court play with flex screen, screen-the-screener, and multiple open shot options; recommended for high school and up.
- [Play flip gate](play-flip-gate.md) — 1-4 high half-court play using a deceptive back screen for a rim cut and a gate screen for the best shooter's catch-and-shoot.
- [Play inside isolate](play-inside-isolate.md) — 4-out 1-in play isolating the best post mismatch at the low block; perimeter screen exchanges keep defenders occupied.
- [Play iverson ram](play-iverson-ram.md) — 1-4 high set play: Iverson wing exchange leads into a ram screen (down screen for the PnR screener) and pick-and-roll with wide-open space.
- [Play piston elevator](play-piston-elevator.md) — 1-4 high play: Iverson cut decoy followed by an elevator screen through the posts, freeing the best shooter for a top-of-key catch-and-shoot three.
- [Play side blaze](play-side-blaze.md) — Horns set play using a wing dribble hand-off followed immediately by a PnR; weak-side screen exchange removes help defenders from the key.
- [Play high-post double curls](play-double-curls.md) — 1-4 high play: High-Post cut and staggered screen send two guards curling to the rim for layups, with wing PnR as the third option.
- [Play high-post double screen](play-high-post-double-screen.md) — 1-4 high play: PG makes a High-Post cut for layup, then a wing PnR frees PG off a weak-side double screen for a catch-and-shoot.
- [Play x cross](play-x-cross.md) — High 2-3 formation play: simultaneous guard X-cuts off the post create layup reads, then flex and staggered screens produce a top-of-key catch-and-shoot.
- [Blob belmont flash](blob-belmont-flash.md) — BLOB vs 2-3 zone (wide box set): flash to mid-key, screen on ball-side post, in-bounder curls to corner for open 3.
- [Blob box flash](blob-box-flash.md) — BLOB vs 2-3 zone (box set): zone overload with double screen for shooter; multiple options including backdoor and wing 3.
- [Blob cross](blob-cross.md) — BLOB vs 2-3 zone (1-4 high): simple crossing action forces 3 defenders to cover 4 players — ideal for youth teams.
- [Blob double skip](blob-double-skip.md) — BLOB vs 2-3 zone (1-4 high): two skip passes shift the zone side-to-side; double flare screens free in-bounder for open wing 3.
- [Blob hawk](blob-hawk.md) — BLOB vs 2-3 zone (irregular formation): dual simultaneous screens force low defender choice — corner 3 or low-block midrange.
- [Blob side cross elevator](blob-side-cross-elevator.md) — BLOB vs 2-3 zone (box shifted ball-side): sequential elevator screens by both post players free best shooter in strong-side corner.
- [Blob stack zone](blob-stack-zone.md) — BLOB vs 2-3 zone: stack formation clears low defenders, creating gap for midrange shot or corner 3.
- [Blob 4 low flex](blob-4-low-flex.md) — BLOB man-to-man play from 4-low formation using flex screen and screen-the-screener for layup or catch-and-shoot.
- [Blob box gate](blob-box-gate.md) — BLOB man play from box: shooter sets back screen for center's layup, then uses gate screen for wing catch-and-shoot.
- [Blob flip](blob-flip.md) — BLOB man play from box: cross screen frees two post players to attack the rim simultaneously for open layups.
- [Blob stack double](blob-stack-double.md) — BLOB man play: stack formation with staggered double screen frees best shooter for wing midrange or three-pointer.
- [Blob stack man](blob-stack-man.md) — Simple youth BLOB from stack: sequential hard cuts spread the court and open the third-in-line player for a near-basket shot.
- [Blob two inside](blob-two-inside.md) — BLOB man play from box using screen-the-screener to feed either post player at the rim; guards occupy perimeter defenders.
- [Blob yo yo](blob-yo-yo.md) — Simple box BLOB: guards set simultaneous up-screens for two post players who cut to the rim for layups.
- [23 flare](23-flare.md) — Set play vs 2-3 zone: ball movement draws zone defenders, then a quick flare screen frees the best shooter for an open three.
- [32 lob](32-lob.md) — Set play vs 2-3 zone: defense is overloaded to one side then a weak-side screen springs an athletic player for a backdoor lob.
- [Play zipper curl](play-zipper-curl.md) — 1-4 high SLOB play using zipper cut and single/double screens to free best shooter for wing jump shot.
- [Play box loop post](play-box-loop-post.md) — SLOB box-set play using sequential down screens to isolate the best post player at the high post 1-on-1.
- [Play box spin](play-box-spin.md) — SLOB box-set quick hitter with double screens sending a cutter to the rim and a shooter to the three-point line.
- [Play deception slob](play-deception-slob.md) — SLOB box-set play creating simultaneous backdoor layup for the inbounder and three-point shot for the best shooter.
- [Play diamond slob](play-diamond-slob.md) — SLOB box-set play with multiple scoring options: curl cut, flare screen three, and pick-and-roll for best playmaker.
- [Play loop fly slob](play-loop-fly-slob.md) — SLOB wide-box play featuring an alley-oop to a post player off a back screen, with a secondary layup option.
- [Play option slob](play-option-slob.md) — SLOB box-set play where the best shooter reads their defender and chooses to cut top or baseline for a catch-and-shoot.
- [Play prowl slob](play-prowl-slob.md) — Quick SLOB box-set play flowing directly into a pick-and-roll at the top of the key with good floor spacing.
- [Play triangle slob](play-triangle-slob.md) — SLOB play using cross-screen and screen-the-screener action to create a low-post opportunity or perimeter catch-and-shoot.
- [Slob twist](slob-twist.md) — SLOB 'Twist' — box formation with lob option, ram screen, and PG attacking the paint off an on-ball screen.
- [Slob x](slob-x.md) — SLOB 'X' — box formation with staggered screens sending two shooters to the wings for mid-range or three-point looks.

## Source Summaries
- [Source youth basketball drills](source-youth-basketball-drills.md) — Youth Basketball Drills (2nd ed.) by Burrall & Patrick Paye — 160 progressive drills for ages 6-14 covering all offensive and defensive fundamentals from beginner through advanced.
- [Source winning basketball fundamentals](source-winning-basketball-fundamentals.md) — Winning Basketball Fundamentals by Lee Rose (2013, Human Kinetics) — 9-chapter fundamentals guide covering guiding principles, performance rating, individual/team offense, defense, and special situations from college and NBA coaching.
- [Source basketball playbook 2](source-basketball-playbook-2.md) — Basketball Playbook 2 — Ociepka & Ratermann (2001): all-new NBA offensive plays organized by scouting category — early offense, post-ups, PnR, baseline screens, 1-4 high, combination plays, and OOB actions.
- [Source basketball sports medicine science](source-basketball-sports-medicine-science.md) — Basketball Sports Medicine and Science (S10, ESSKA 2020) — 81-chapter medical/science encyclopedia covering physiology, anthropometrics, game demands, injury prevention, rehabilitation, strength training, psychology, and special populations.
- [Source basketball sports medicine](source-basketball-sports-medicine-science.md) — Basketball Sports Medicine and Science (ESSKA, 2020) — eds. Laver et al. — comprehensive clinical reference covering all major basketball injuries and rehabilitation from ACL to foot/ankle to tendinopathy
- [Source strength training basketball nsca](source-strength-training-basketball-nsca.md) — Strength Training for Basketball (NSCA, 2020) — eds. Gillett & Burgos — science-based resistance training guide covering program design, exercise technique, and periodized sample programs for basketball athletes.
- [Source improving practice performance basketball](source-improving-practice-performance-basketball.md) — Improving Practice and Performance in Basketball (S12) — MDPI Sports special issue: 10 research studies on fatigue monitoring, workload management, game statistics, body composition, and player development.
- [Source improving practice performance](source-improving-practice-performance-basketball.md) — Improving Practice Performance Basketball (S12) — academic journal collection covering athlete monitoring, fatigue management, performance indicators, and training load in basketball.
- [Source nba coaches playbook](source-coaches-playbook.md) — pro Coaches Playbook — NBCA (S7): 21-chapter encyclopedia of pro coaching knowledge covering individual offense, team offense, fast break, special plays, defense, and coaching essentials from 30+ pro coaches.
- [Source explosive calisthenics](source-explosive-calisthenics.md) — Explosive Calisthenics — Superhuman Power, Maximum Speed and Agility (S9) — progressive calisthenics manual covering back flip, front flip, handspring, and explosive bodyweight training chains for total athletic development.
- [Source footwork balance pivoting](source-footwork-balance-pivoting.md) — The Complete Basketball Coaches Guide to Footwork, Balance, and Pivoting (S6) — comprehensive footwork system covering pivoting, catching, screening, dribbling, driving, trapping, and footwork-based drills for all offensive and defensive situations.
- [Source speed agility quickness](source-speed-agility-quickness.md) — Training for Speed, Agility, and Quickness (2nd ed.) by Brown & Ferrigno — 195-drill SAQ training manual covering muscle physiology, assessment, speed, agility, balance, quickness, reaction time, and sport-specific program design.
- [Source lets talk defense](source-lets-talk-defense.md) — Let's Talk Defense! by Herb Brown — comprehensive defensive basketball guide covering philosophy, principles, drills, individual/team defense, pick-and-roll, trapping, transition, zone, press, scouting, and more.
- [Source herb brown defense](source-herb-brown-defense.md) — Let's Talk Defense by Herb Brown — comprehensive man-to-man and team defense system covering individual skills, help defense, transition, press, zone, and combination defenses.
- [Source offensive skill development](source-offensive-skill-development.md) — Basketball Coaches' Guide to Advanced Offensive Skill Development (S3) — comprehensive individual offensive skill system covering shooting mechanics, live-ball moves, drills, and structured workout programs.
- [Source basketball anatomy](source-basketball-anatomy.md) — Basketball Anatomy by Brian Cole & Rob Panariello — illustrated guide to basketball-specific strength, power, plyometrics, rehabilitation, and injury prevention.
- [Source basketball shooting](source-basketball-shooting.md) — Basketball Shooting by the shooting specialist — comprehensive shooting guide covering philosophy, visualization, technique, free throws, jump shots, bank shots, creating shots, and screens.
- [Source basketball for coaches](source-basketball-for-coaches.md) — 50 Basketball Plays by Coach Mac (Trevor McLean) — BLOB, SLOB, set plays vs man and zone for all levels.
